这里的 \(u_{0}(t,x)\) 相应于用分离变量法求解时将边界条件齐次化的特解。在用Laplace变换求解时，对于非齐次边界条件不需要作特殊处理，这是它的优点，当然随之而来的是求反变换的麻烦。

基本解方法¶

一个偏微分方程通常反映了某个物理场和引起这个场的场源之间的关系。最简单的场源是点源，连续分布的场源则可看成点源的叠加。对于线性偏微分方程，如果知道点源产生的场（称为基本解或点源函数），便可以通过线性叠加原理求出相应连续源产生的场，这就是基本解方法。由于点源的特殊性，基本解有可能用较简单、特殊的方法求得。因此，基本解方法成为求解线性偏微分方程的重要方法之一。

delta函数，广义函数简介¶

delta函数和广义函数¶

描述一个在空间连续分布的物理量 \(Q\) ，通常有两种方式。一种是局部性的，给出密度函数分布 \(\rho(M)=\frac{\mathrm{d}Q}{\mathrm{d}M},~ M\in\mathbb{R}^{n}(n=1,2,3)\) ；另一种是整体性的，通过空间任意区域 \(\Omega \subset \mathbb{R}^{n}\) 该物理量的总量

\[\begin{align} Q(\Omega) = \int_{\Omega}\rho(M)~\mathrm{d}M \end{align}\]

给出。对于集中分布的物理量，也可以通过这两种方式来表述。我们先来讨论集中分布物理量的密度函数。

注解

考虑点电荷的线密度。直线 \(L\) 上仅在 \(x=0\) 处放置一单位电荷，这可以看成是单位电荷均匀分布在小区间 \([-\varepsilon, \varepsilon]\) 上当 \(\varepsilon \to 0\) 时的极限情况。后者的密度

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \rho_{\varepsilon} = \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \frac{1}{2\varepsilon} ,\quad |x| \le \varepsilon \\ 0 ,\quad |x| > \varepsilon \end{array} \right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

且 \(\forall \varepsilon > 0\) ，直线上的电荷总量

\[\begin{align} Q = \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\rho_{\varepsilon}(x)~\mathrm{d}x = 1 \end{align}\]

令 \(\varepsilon \to 0\) ，可由 \(\rho_{\varepsilon}(x)\) 的极限推得单位点电荷的分布

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \rho(x) = \left\{ \begin{array}{l} +\infty ,\quad x=0 \\ 0 ,\quad x\ne 0 \end{array} \right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

且保持直线上的电荷总量为 \(1\) 。

将集中于 \(x=0\) 点的单位物理量引起的密度函数成为 \(\delta\) 函数，记为 \(\delta(x)\) ，即 \(\delta(x)\) 满足条件

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \delta(x) = \left\{ \begin{array}{l} +\infty ,\quad x=0 \\ 0 ,\quad x\ne 0 \end{array} \right. ,\qquad \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\delta(x)~\mathrm{d}x = 1 \end{align}\end{split}\]

置于 \(x=\xi\) 点的单位物理量引起的密度函数可以用 \(\delta(x)\) 的平移 \(\delta(x-\xi)\) 表示

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \delta(x-\xi) = \left\{ \begin{array}{l} +\infty ,\quad x=\xi \\ 0 ,\quad x\ne \xi \end{array} \right. ,\qquad \int_{-\infty}^{\infty}\delta(x-\xi)~\mathrm{d}x = 1 \end{align}\end{split}\]

注解

考虑点热源产生的温度分布。温度为 \(0\) 的均匀导热细杆，线密度为 \(\rho\) ，比热为 \(c\) 。在某一瞬间给 \(x=\xi\) 点热量 \(Q\) ，在加热的瞬间，热量尚未传播出去，在 \(x\ne \xi\) 处，瞬时温度保持为 \(T(x) = 0\) ；而在加热点 \(\xi\) 处，加热瞬间温度上升

\[\begin{align} T(\xi) = \lim_{\Delta x\to +0}\frac{Q}{c \rho\Delta x} = +\infty \end{align}\]

整根杆上使温度增加的热量是确定的

\[\begin{align} \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}c\rho T(x)~\mathrm{d}x = Q \end{align}\]

对比 \(\delta\) 函数的定义式，加热瞬时杆上的温度分布

\[\begin{align} T(x) = \frac{Q}{c\rho}\delta(x - \xi) \end{align}\]

注解

考虑冲量一定的顺时力。在 \(t=\tau\) 瞬间，有冲量一定的顺时力作用在质量为 \(m\) 的静止小球上，小球产生速度为 \(v\) 的匀速直线运动。显然，当 \(t\ne \tau\) 时，小球所受外力 \(F(t)=0\) 。在 \(t=\tau\) 瞬间，小球得到动量

\[\begin{align} mv = \lim_{\Delta t \to +0} F(\tau)\Delta t \end{align}\]

因此，在 \(t=\tau\) 瞬时，小球所受的外力 \(F(\tau)\) 应该为 \(+\infty\) 。又由动量守恒原理可知，在整个过程中

\[\begin{align} mv = \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}F(t)~\mathrm{d}t \end{align}\]

所以，小球所受的外力

\[\begin{align} F(t) = mv\delta(t-\tau) \end{align}\]

无论是关于空间还是关于时间集中分布的物理量都可以用 \(\delta\) 函数来描述。关于时间集中分布的物理量在实际问题中常称为脉冲。

\(\delta\) 函数有一条非常重要的基本性质，应用上称为 筛选性 ，即对任意 \(\varphi(x) \in C(\mathbb{R})\) ，

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \int_{a}^{b}\delta(x)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x = \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \varphi(0) ,\quad 0 \in [a,b] \\ 0 ,\quad 0 \notin [a,b] \end{array} \right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

特别地

\[\begin{align} \int_{-\infty}^{\infty}\delta(x)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x = \varphi(0) \end{align}\]

也可以这样看，由于当 \(x\ne 0\) 时 \(\delta(x)=0\) ，故

\[\begin{align} \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\delta(x)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x = \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\delta(x)\varphi(0)~\mathrm{d}x = \varphi(0) \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\delta(x)~\mathrm{d}x = \varphi(0) \end{align}\]

\(\delta(x-\xi)\) 的筛选性为

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \int_{a}^{b}\delta(x-\xi)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x = \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \varphi(\xi) ,\quad \xi \in [a,b] \\ 0 ,\quad \xi \notin [a,b] \end{array} \right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

特别地

\[\begin{align} \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\delta(x-\xi)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x = \varphi(\xi) \end{align}\]

筛选性表达式就是集中分布物理量的另一种数学描述。当 \(\varphi(x)=1\) 时，筛选性说明，只要区间里包含 \(x=0\) 点，该区间内此物理量的总量为 \(1\) ，否则总量为 \(0\) 。对于一般的 \(\varphi(x)\) ，筛选性表达式是 \(\varphi(x)\) 在 \([a,b]\) 上以 \(\delta(x)\) 为权函数的加权平均，同样反映了 \(\delta(x)\) 的集中分布性。所以，也可以把筛选性作为 \(\delta(x)\) 的另一种定义。

选用筛选性作为 \(\delta(x)\) 的定义则可以对其产生一种全新认识。 \(\delta\) 函数实际上是一个映射，它把 \(C(\mathbb{R})\) 中的元素 \(\varphi(x)\) 映成了 \(\mathbb{R}\) 中的一个数 \(\varphi(0)\) 。称函数空间到数域的线性映射为函数空间上的一个线性泛函，则 \(\delta\) 函数就是 \(C(\mathbb{R})\) 上的一个特殊的线性泛函，用内积或积分形式记 \(\delta\) 函数对应的泛函值，即

\[\begin{align} \left \langle \delta(x), \varphi(x) \right \rangle = \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\delta(x)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x = \varphi(0) \end{align}\]

如果一个只在有限区间上不为 \(0\) 的可积函数 \(f(x)\) ，则由

\[\begin{align} \left \langle f(x),\varphi(x) \right \rangle = \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}f(x)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x \end{align}\]

也确定了一个 \(C(\mathbb{R})\) 上的线性泛函。所以，从线性泛函的角度， \(\delta(x)\) 和 \(f(x)\) 并无二异。

称 \(C(\mathbb{R})\) 上的线性泛函为 广义函数 ，线性泛函的全体构成一个广义函数空间，记为 \(C'(\mathbb{R})\) ，称为基本函数空间 \(C(\mathbb{R})\) 的对偶空间。上述 \(\delta(x), f(x)\) 均为广义函数，称 \(\delta(x)\) 为奇异广义函数，称 \(f(x)\) 为正则广义函数。

基本函数空间可以是不同的，定义在其上的线性泛函的全体构成的广义函数空间也就不同。例如，基本函数空间是 \(C^{\infty}(\mathbb{R})\) 时，与其对偶的广义函数空间就记为 \((C^{\infty}(\mathbb{R}))'\) ，上述 \(\delta(x), f(x)\) 也都是此空间中的广义函数。以后常常用 \(\varphi(x), \varphi_{n}(x), \psi(x)\) 等表示基本函数空间中的函数，而广义函数空间中的广义函数常常用 \(f(x),f_{n}(x),g(x)\) 等表示。

delta函数和广义函数的性质和运算¶

对称性¶
\[\begin{align} \delta(x-\xi) = \delta(\xi - x) ,\quad \text{特别地，有} \quad \delta(x)=\delta(-x) \end{align}\]

这是由于 \(\forall \varphi(x) \in C(\mathbb{R})\) ，

\[\begin{align} \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\delta(\xi - x)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x = \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\delta(u)\varphi(\xi - u)~\mathrm{d}u = \varphi(\xi - u)|_{u=0} = \varphi(\xi) \end{align}\]

与 \(\delta(x-\xi)\) 对 \(\varphi(x)\) 的筛选作用相同。

\(\delta\) 函数与连续函数的乘积¶

对于连续函数 \(a(x)\) ，有

\[\begin{align} a(x) \delta(x-\xi) = a(\xi)\delta(x - \xi) \end{align}\]

这是因为 \(\forall \varphi(x) \in C(\mathbb{R})\) ，

\[\begin{align} \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}a(x)\delta(x-\xi)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x = \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\delta(x-\xi)[a(x)\varphi(x)]~\mathrm{d}x = a(\xi)\varphi(\xi) \end{align}\]
\[\begin{align} \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}a(\xi)\delta(x-\xi)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x = a(\xi)\int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\delta(x-\xi)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x = a(\xi)\varphi(\xi) \end{align}\]

可以看到，当 \(a(\xi)=0\) 时，不定式 \(a(x)\delta(x-\xi)=0\) 。例如，我们有 \(x^{n}\delta(x)=0,~n=1,2,\cdots\) 。

\(\delta\) 函数与普通函数的复合¶

设 \(u(x) \in C^{1}(\mathbb{R})\) ，且在实轴上只有单零点 \(x_{k}(k=1,2,\cdots,N)\) ，则复合函数

\[\begin{align} \delta(u(x)) = \sum_{k=1}^{N}\frac{\delta(x-x_{k})}{|u'(x_{k})|} \end{align}\]

可以这样看， \(\forall \varphi(x) \in C(\mathbb{R})\) ，由于 \(u(x_{k})=0~(k=1,2,\cdots,N)\) ，有

\[\begin{align} \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\delta[u(x)]\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x = \sum_{k=1}^{N}\int_{x_{k}-\varepsilon_{k}}^{x_{k}+\varepsilon_{k}}\delta[u(x)]\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x \end{align}\]

其中 \(\varepsilon_{k}\) 为小正数。又由于 \(u'(x_{k}) \ne 0\) 及 \(u'(x)\) 连续，总可以将相应的 \(\varepsilon_{k}\) 取得足够小，使 \(u'(x)\) 在积分区间 \([x_{k}-\varepsilon_{k}, x_{k}+\varepsilon_{k}]\) 上不变号。不妨假设 \(u'(x_{k})<0\) ，则 \(u(x)\) 在此区间上严格单调下降。作变量代换 \(u=u(x)\) ，记 \(u_{1} = u(x_{k}+\varepsilon_{k}), u_{2} = u(x_{k}-\varepsilon_{k})\) ，有 \(u_{1} < 0 < u_{2}\) ，所以

\[\begin{align} \int_{x_{k}-\varepsilon_{k}}^{x_{k}+\varepsilon_{k}}\delta[u(x)]\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x = - \int_{u_{1}}^{u_{2}}\delta(u)\varphi(x(u))x'(u)~\mathrm{d}u = \int_{u_{1}}^{u_{2}}\delta(u)\frac{\varphi(x(u))}{-u'(x)}~\mathrm{d}u = \frac{\varphi(x(u))}{|u'(x(u))|}\Big|_{u=0} = \frac{\varphi(x_{k})}{|u'(x_{k})|} \end{align}\]

而我们所考虑的复合函数公式右边的每一项对 \(\varphi(x)\) 的作用也得到

\[\begin{align} \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\frac{\delta(x-x_{k})}{|u'(x_{k})|}\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x = \frac{\varphi(x_{k})}{|u'(x_{k})|} \end{align}\]

注解

利用复合公式可以得到很多有用的结果，例如

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} & \delta(ax) = \frac{\delta(x)}{|a|} \\ & \delta(x^{2}-a^{2}) = \frac{\delta(x-a)}{2|a|} + \frac{\delta(x+a)}{2|a|} = \frac{\delta(x-a)}{2|x|} + \frac{\delta(x+a)}{2|x|} \\ & \delta(\sin x) = \sum_{k=-\infty}^{+\infty}\delta(x-k\pi) \\ & |x|\delta(x^{2}) = \lim_{a\to 0}|x|\delta(x^{2}-a^{2}) = \delta(x) \end{align}\end{split}\]
\(\delta\) 函数和广义函数的导数¶

为了使 \(\delta\) 函数和一般的广义函数无穷次可导，也为了扩大广义函数的范围，就要使基本函数空间具有 \(C^{\infty}(\mathbb{R})\) 的光滑性且还要有其他较强的性质，为此引入 \(C_{0}^{\infty}(\mathbb{R})\) （或者记为 \(\mathscr{D}(\mathbb{R})\) ）基本函数空间，它包含的函数 \(\varphi(x)\) 是无穷次连续可导而且在一个有界的闭区间外为零。例如，最典型的是下面这类函数

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \varphi(x) = b(x)\eta(x,a) ,\quad \eta(x,a) = \left\{ \begin{array}{l} e^{\frac{1}{x^{2}-a^{2}}} ,\quad |x|<a \\ 0 ,\quad |x| \ge a \end{array} \right. ,\quad b(x) \in C^{\infty}(\mathbb{R}) \end{align}\end{split}\]

定义在 \(\mathscr{D}(\mathbb{R})\) 上线性泛函的全体构成一个广义函数空间 \(\mathscr{D}'(\mathbb{R})\) ， \(\delta(x)\) 是其中一个奇异广义函数，任何一个局部可积的函数 \(f(x)\) 均为正则广义函数，它们的泛函值分别为

\[\begin{align} \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\delta(x)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x = \varphi(0) ,\qquad \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}f(x)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x \end{align}\]

如果 \(f(x)\) 是 \(\mathscr{D}'(\mathbb{R})\) 中的广义函数，则 \(f^{(n)}(x)\) 也是一个广义函数，其定义为

\[\begin{align} \left \langle f^{(n)}(x), \varphi(x) \right \rangle := (-1)^{n} \left \langle f(x), \varphi^{(n)}(x) \right \rangle ,\quad \forall \varphi(x) \in C_{0}^{\infty}(\mathbb{R}) \end{align}\]

用积分的形式来表示即为

\[\begin{align} \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}f^{(n)}(x)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x := (-1)^{n}\int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}f(x)\varphi^{(n)}(x)~\mathrm{d}x \end{align}\]

在形式上相当于进行分部积分，把对广义函数的求导运算转移到基本函数上，特别地

\[\begin{align} \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\delta^{(n)}(x)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x = (-1)^{n}\int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\delta(x)\varphi^{(n)}(x)~\mathrm{d}x = (-1)^{n}\varphi^{(n)}(0) \end{align}\]

这样，任何一个广义函数均是无穷次可导的，特别地任何一个连续函数 \(f(x)\) 是无穷次可导的。

广义函数的原函数和 \(\delta\) 函数的原函数¶

如果 \(g'(x)=f(x)\) ，则称 \(g(x)\) 是 \(f(x)\) 的一个原函数，这时 \(g(x)+C\) 也是 \(f(x)\) 的原函数。特别地，不难直接证明 \(H'(x) = \delta(x)\) ，即 \(H(x)\) 是 \(\delta(x)\) 的一个原函数。这个结果形式上也可以从 \(\delta(x)\) 变上限积分得到，即

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \int_{-\infty}^{x}\delta(x)~\mathrm{d}x = \left\{ \begin{array}{l} 0 ,\quad x<0 \\ 1 ,\quad x\ge 0 \end{array} \right. \quad= H(x) \end{align}\end{split}\]

根据原函数的概念，要求 \(\delta(x)\) 的原函数就是要求微分方程 \(y'(x) = \delta(x)\) 的解，方程的通解为 \(H(x) + C\) ，如果取 \(C=-\frac{1}{2}\) ，可以得到 \(\delta(x)\) 的另一个函数 \(\frac{1}{2}\operatorname{sgn}x\) 。

广义函数的卷积、 \(\delta\) 函数和广义函数的卷积¶

如果 \(f(x), g(x)\) 为两个广义函数，则卷积 \(h(x) = f(x)*g(x)\) 定义了一个广义函数 \(h(x)\) 如下：

\[\begin{align} \left \langle h(x),\varphi(x) \right \rangle := \left \langle f(x), \left\langle g(y), \varphi(x+y) \right\rangle \right \rangle \end{align}\]

即用累次泛函来定义。广义函数的卷积仍形式地记为

\[\begin{align} f(x)*g(x) = \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}f(\xi)g(x-\xi)~\mathrm{d}\xi \end{align}\]

如果形式地交换积分的顺序并进行变数代换，得到

\[\begin{align} \langle h(x), \varphi(x) \rangle = \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}f(\xi)~\mathrm{d}\xi \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}g(u)\varphi(\xi+u)~\mathrm{d}u = \langle f(x), \langle g(y), \varphi(x+y) \rangle \rangle \end{align}\]

特别地，不难得到

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} & \delta(x) * f(x) = f(x) \\ & \delta'(x) * f(x) = \delta(x) * f'(x) = f'(x) \\ & \delta^{(n)}(x) * f(x) = \delta(x) * f^{(n)}(x) = f^{(n)}(x) \\ & L(f(x) * g(x)) = (Lf) * g = f * (Lg) \end{align}\end{split}\]

其中， \(L\) 是常系数线性微分算子。

广义函数和 \(\delta\) 函数的Fourier变换¶

为了自由地进行广义函数的 \(FT\) 和 \(F^{-1}T\) 又需要引入另一个基本函数空间 \(\varphi(\mathbb{R})\) ，它的函数 \(\varphi(x)\) 是无穷次连续可导且是速降的，即对于任意非负整数 \(m\) 和 \(n\) ，当 \(|x| \to +\infty\) 时， \(x^{m}\varphi^{(n)}(x) \to 0\) 。这种函数最典型的一类是 \(p(x)e^{-ax^{2}}~(a>0)\) ，其中 \(p(x)\) 是 \(x\) 的多项式。在 \(\varphi(\mathbb{R})\) 上线性泛函的全体构成一个对偶的广义函数空间 \(\varphi'(\mathbb{R})\) ， \(\delta(x)\) 也是它的奇异广义函数、任意一个局部可积的函数 \(f(x)\) ，且当 \(|x| \to \infty\) 时 \(f(x)\) 的增长不超过一个多项式，这时 \(f(x)\) 是 \(\varphi'(\mathbb{R})\) 的正则广义函数。

如果 \(f(x) \in \varphi'(\mathbb{R})\) ，则 \(F[f], F^{-1}[f]\) 也是广义函数，定义如下：

\[\begin{align} \langle F[f], \varphi \rangle := \langle f, F[\varphi] \rangle ,\qquad \langle F^{-1}[f], \varphi \rangle := \langle f, F^{-1}[\varphi] \rangle \end{align}\]

即把 \(FT\) 和 \(F^{-1}T\) 转移到基本函数上。广义函数的 \(FT\) 和 \(F^{-1}T\) 仍记为

\[\begin{align} F[f] = \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}f(x)e^{-\mathrm{i} \lambda x}~\mathrm{d}x = \hat{f}(\lambda) ,\quad F^{-1}[f] = \frac{1}{2\pi}\int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}f(\lambda)e^{\mathrm{i}\lambda x}~\mathrm{d}\lambda \end{align}\]

这样， \(FT\) 建立了 \(\varphi'(\mathbb{R})\) 中广义函数之间一一对应的关系

\[\begin{align} f(x) \overset{FT}{\underset{F^{-1}T}{\rightleftharpoons}} \hat{f}(\lambda) \end{align}\]

而且保持着 \(FT\) 的基本性质：线性性质、微分性质、像函数的微分性质、平移性质、频移性质、相似性质、反射性质和卷积性质。根据这些性质由某几个特殊的广义函数的 \(FT\) 就能得出许多广义函数的 \(FT\) 。特别地由于

\[\begin{align} F[\delta(x)] = \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\delta(x)e^{-\mathrm{i}\lambda x}~\mathrm{d}x = 1 \end{align}\]

可以得到

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} & 1 \overset{FT}{\underset{F^{-1}T}{\rightleftharpoons}} 2\pi \delta(\lambda) \\ & e^{\mathrm{i}ax} \rightleftharpoons 2\pi \delta(\lambda - a) \\ & \cos ax \rightleftharpoons \pi [\delta(\lambda + a) + \delta(\lambda - a)] \\ & \sin ax \rightleftharpoons \mathrm{i}\pi [\delta(\lambda + a) - \delta(\lambda - a)] \\ & x \rightleftharpoons 2\pi \mathrm{i}\delta'(\lambda) \end{align}\end{split}\]

如果用积分形式来表示，可以得到

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} & \int_{-\infty}^{\infty} e^{\pm \mathrm{i}\lambda x}~\mathrm{d}x = 2\pi \delta(\lambda) \\ & \int_{-\infty}^{\infty} \cos\lambda x~\mathrm{d}x = 2\pi \delta(\lambda) \\ & \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}x e^{-\mathrm{i}\lambda x}~\mathrm{d}x = 2\pi \mathrm{i}\delta'(\lambda) \end{align}\end{split}\]
delta函数的Fourier展开¶

当 \(x,\xi \in (-\pi, \pi)\) 时

\[\begin{align} \delta(x - \xi) = \frac{a_{0}}{2} + \sum_{n=1}^{+\infty}(a_{n}\cos nx + b_{n}\sin nx) \end{align}\]

其中Fourier系数为

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} & a_{n} = \frac{1}{\pi} \int_{-\pi}^{\pi}\delta(x - \xi)\cos nx~\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{\pi}\cos n\xi \\ & b_{n} = \frac{1}{\pi} \int_{-\pi}^{\pi}\delta(x - \xi)\sin nx~\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{\pi}\sin n\xi \end{align}\end{split}\]

对于其他的正交基， \(\delta\) 函数同样可以作广义Fourier展开。

广义函数序列的收敛性和delta序列¶

设 \(f_{n}(x)\) 为一个广义函数的序列， \(f(x)\) 为一个广义函数，如果对于基本函数空间上的任意函数 \(\varphi(x)\) 均有

\[\begin{align} \lim_{n\to\infty} \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}f_{n}(x)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{d}x = \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}f(x)\varphi(x)~\mathrm{dx} \end{align}\]

则称 \(\lim\limits_{n \to \infty}f_{n}(x) \overset{w}{=} f(x)\) ，这种收敛称为弱收敛和弱极限。特别地，弱收敛于 \(\delta\) 函数的序列称为 \(\delta\) 序列，典型的几个 \(\delta\) 序列为：

  • 矩形脉冲序列： \(\lim\limits_{\varepsilon \to 0^{+}}\rho_{\varepsilon}(x) \overset{w}{=} \delta(x)\) ；
  • Cauchy脉冲序列： \(\lim\limits_{\varepsilon \to 0^{+}}\frac{\varepsilon}{\pi(x^{2} + \varepsilon^{2})} \overset{w}{=} \delta(x)\) ；
  • Gauss脉冲序列： \(\lim\limits_{\varepsilon \to 0^{+}}\frac{1}{\sqrt{2\pi} t}e^{-\frac{x^{2}}{2t^{2}}} \overset{w}{=} \delta(x)\) ；
  • 采样脉冲序列： \(\lim\limits_{N \to +\infty}\frac{\sin Nx}{\pi x} \overset{w}{=} \delta(x)\) 。

直观地看，这些函数列趋于 \(\delta(x)\) ，而且其中每一个函数在实轴上的积分为 \(1\) 。严格的证明需要从弱收敛定义出发。

利用 \(\delta\) 序列可以验证Fourier反变换公式。例如，由采样脉冲序列可知

\[\begin{align} F^{-1}[1] = \frac{1}{2\pi}\int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}e^{\mathrm{i}\lambda x}~\mathrm{d}\lambda = \lim_{N \to +\infty}\frac{1}{2\pi}\int_{-N}^{N}e^{\mathrm{i}\lambda x}~\mathrm{d}\lambda = \lim_{N \to +\infty}\frac{\sin Nx}{\pi x} \overset{w}{=} \delta(x) \end{align}\]

另外，不难证明 \(\lim\limits_{n \to \infty}\sin nx \overset{w}{=} 0\) ， \(\lim\limits_{n \to \infty}\cos nx \overset{w}{=} 0\) 。前面所述的 \(\delta(x)\) 的Fourier级数展开也是在弱收敛意义下的展开式，有时弱收敛也用通常的记号表示。

高维delta函数和广义函数¶

Lu=0型方程的基本解¶

这里讨论用基本解方法求解方程

\[\begin{align} Lu = f(x,y,z) ,\quad -\infty< x,y,z < +\infty \end{align}\]

其中 \(L\) 是关于 \(x,y,z\) 的常系数线性偏微分算子。现在可以把 \(u\) 和 \(f\) 均作为广义函数，在广义函数空间中可以较自由地进行各种运算和变换来求得方程的解，这种解是广义函数，称之为广义解。通常这种解是一个正则广义函数，甚至还有足够的光滑性，那么这种解就称为古典解。当方程的右端为 \(\delta(x,y,z)\) 时，所得的解 \(U(x,y,z)\) 称为方程的基本解，其物理意义就是由点源而产生的物理场。根据基本解可以得出一般的右端函数所对应的解，即一般的源所对应的物理场。基本解不但数学上讨论较为容易，而且有时可以根据问题的物理意义求出。

基本解和解的积分表达式¶

以场位方程为例

\[\begin{align} \Delta_{3}u = f(M) ,\quad M=(x,y,z) \in \mathbb{R}^{3} \end{align}\]

这里 \(f(M) = -\frac{\rho(M)}{\varepsilon}\) ， \(\rho(M)\) 为空间电荷分布， \(\varepsilon\) 为介电常数。

由 \(\delta\) 函数与广义函数的卷积运算，有

\[\begin{align} f(M) = \delta(M) * f(M) = \int_{\mathbb{R}^{3}}\delta(M - M_{0})f(M_{0})\mathrm{d}M_{0} \end{align}\]

这说明一般源 \(f(M)\) 可以看成置于 \(M_{0}\) 点的点源 \(f(M_{0})\delta(M - M_{0})\) 的积分叠加。由积分叠加原理可知，只要求出方程

\[\begin{align} \Delta_{3}V = \delta(M - M_{0}) ,\quad M=(x,y,z),~ M_{0}=(\xi,\eta,\zeta) \in \mathbb{R}^{3} \end{align}\]

的解 \(V(M;M_{0})\) ，便可以得到原方程的解

\[\begin{align} u(M) = \int_{\mathbb{R}^{3}}V(M;M_{0})f(M_{0})~\mathrm{d}M_{0} \end{align}\]

由于在全空间求解，不妨先求解方程

\[\begin{align} \Delta_{3}U = \delta(M) ,\quad M\in\mathbb{R}^{3} \end{align}\]

如果上式的解为 \(U(M)\) ，则平移可以得到 \(V(M;M_{0}) = U(M - M_{0})\) ，进而有

\[\begin{align} u(M) = \int_{\mathbb{R}^{3}}U(M-M_{0})f(M_{0})~\mathrm{d}M_{0} = U(M) * f(M) \end{align}\]

该公式反映了一般的源产生的是点源产生场的叠加。这里起基本作用的是置于原点的点源 \(\delta(M)\) 产生的场 \(U(M)\) ，称它为基本解。一般有如下定义：方程 \(LU = \delta(M)\) 的解 \(U(M)\) 称为 \(Lu=0\) 型方程的基本解，其中 \(L\) 是关于自变量 \(M = (x,y,z)\) 的常系数线性偏微分算子。

由定义可知，基本解是点源产生的场，物理上也称为点源函数。这里的基本解没有定解条件限制，因此不是唯一的，可以相差齐次方程 \(Lu=0\) 的解，通常根据问题的物理意义和数学的需要选定其中一个。基本解满足的方程的右端是 \(\delta(M)\) ，因此基本解已经不是古典解，而是一种广义解。

由基本解可以得到非其次方程 \(Lu = f(M)\) 的解的积分公式。设 \(U(M)\) 是 \(Lu = 0\) 型方程的基本解，则

\[\begin{align} u = U(M) * f(M) = \int_{\mathbb{R}^{3}}U(M-M_{0})f(M_{0})~\mathrm{d}M_{0} \end{align}\]

满足方程

\[\begin{align} Lu = f(M) \end{align}\]

注解

证明如下：由 \(LU(M - M_{0}) = \delta(M - M_{0})\) ，有

\[\begin{align} Lu = L(U(M) * f(M)) = \int_{\mathbb{R}^{3}}LU(M - M_{0})f(M_{0})~\mathrm{d}M_{0} = \int_{\mathbb{R}^{3}}\delta(M - M_{0})f(M_{0})~\mathrm{d}M_{0} = f(M) \end{align}\]

这里我们毫无顾忌地交换了微分和积分的次序，这在经典分析中是不允许的，但是，现在我们求的是广义解，在广义函数理论中广义函数的微分与卷积可以交换次序，形式上便是微分与积分可以任意交换次序。

基本解的求法¶

从数学上求基本解，即在全空间求解方程 \(Lu = \delta(M)\) 。 \(\delta(M)\) 并非普通函数，但由相关的运算和性质，可以像对待普通函数一样求解这个方程。另一方面，由 \(\delta\) 函数的筛选性，也可以采用一些特殊方法求解。

注解

要求常微分方程 \(y' + ay = 0\) 的基本解，这里常数 \(a>0\) ，也即求方程

\[\begin{align} U' + aU = \delta(x) \end{align}\]

的解。将方程两边同乘 \(e^{ax}\) ，得到

\[\begin{align} \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}(e^{ax}U) = e^{ax}\delta(x) = \delta(x) \end{align}\]

由于 \(H'(x) = \delta(x)\) ，取基本解

\[\begin{align} U(x) = e^{-ax}H(x) \end{align}\]

利用解的积分公式，可以得到非齐次方程 \(y'+ay=f(x)\) 的一个解

\[\begin{align} y(x) = U * f(x) = \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}e^{-a\xi}H(\xi)f(x-\xi)~\mathrm{d}\xi = \int_{0}^{+\infty}e^{-a\xi}f(x - \xi)~\mathrm{d}\xi = \int_{-\infty}^{x}e^{-a(x - \xi)}f(\xi)~\mathrm{d}\xi \end{align}\]

注解

求三维Laplace方程的基本解，可以用三维FT求解

\[\begin{align} \Delta_{3}U = \delta(x,y,z) ,\quad -\infty < x,y,z < +\infty \end{align}\]

记 \(\hat{U}(\lambda,\mu,\nu) = F[U(x,y,z)]\) 。由于 \(F[\delta(x,y,z)] = 1\) ，像函数满足代数方程

\[\begin{align} -(\lambda^{2} + \mu^{2} + \nu^{2})\hat{U} = 1 \end{align}\]

解得

\[\begin{align} \hat{U} = -\frac{1}{\rho^{2}} ,\quad \rho^{2} = \lambda^{2} + \mu^{2} + \nu^{2} ,\quad (\lambda,\mu,\nu) \in \mathbb{R}^{3} \end{align}\]

作反变换，得到

\[\begin{align} U = F^{-1}[\hat{U}] = -\frac{1}{(2\pi)^{3}}\iiint\limits_{-\infty}^{+\infty} \frac{1}{\rho^{2}} e^{\mathrm{i}(\lambda x + \mu y + \nu z)}~\mathrm{d}\lambda\mathrm{d}\mu\mathrm{d}\nu = -\frac{1}{(2\pi)^{3}} \iiint\limits_{-\infty}^{+\infty} \frac{1}{\rho^{2}} e^{\mathrm{i}\mathbf{\rho} \cdot \mathbf{r}}~\mathrm{d}\lambda\mathrm{d}\mu\mathrm{d}\nu = -\frac{1}{(2\pi)^{3}} \iiint\limits_{-\infty}^{+\infty} \frac{1}{\rho^{2}} e^{\mathrm{i}\rho r\cos\theta}\mathrm{d}\lambda\mathrm{d}\mu\mathrm{d}\nu \end{align}\]

这里，向量 \(\mathbf{\rho} = (\lambda, \mu, \nu)\) ， \(\mathbf{r} = (x,y,z)\) ， \(r^{2} = x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2}\) ， \(\theta\) 为 \(\mathbf{\rho}\) 与 \(\mathbf{r}\) 的夹角。由于积分区域是全空间，被积函数关于向量 \(\mathbf{r}\) 轴对称，不妨将 \(\nu\) 轴取在 \(\mathbf{r}\) 方向，作球坐标变换

\[\begin{align} \lambda = \rho\sin\theta\cos\varphi ,\quad \mu = \rho\sin\theta\sin\varphi ,\quad \nu = \rho\cos\theta \end{align}\]

得到

\[\begin{align} U(x,y,z) = -\frac{1}{(2\pi)^{3}} \int_{0}^{+\infty}\int_{0}^{\pi}\int_{0}^{2\pi}e^{\mathrm{i}\rho r\cos\theta}\sin\theta~\mathrm{d}\varphi\mathrm{d}\theta\mathrm{d}\rho = \frac{1}{(2\pi)^{2}}\int_{0}^{+\infty} \frac{e^{\mathrm{i}\rho r\cos\theta}}{\mathrm{i}\rho r}\Big|_{0}^{\pi}~\mathrm{d}\rho = -\frac{1}{2\pi^{2}r} \int_{0}^{+\infty}\frac{\sin \rho r}{\rho}~\mathrm{d}\rho = -\frac{1}{4\pi r} \end{align}\]

这个基本解就是置于原点的 \(-\varepsilon\) 电荷在无穷远零电位的条件下在全空间产生的电场。

还可以利用 \(\delta\) 函数的筛选性来求基本解，这需要用到场论里的Green公式。设区域 \(V\) 由分片光滑闭曲面 \(S\) 围成， \(u(M), v(M)\) 在区域 \(V\) 内有二阶连续偏导数，在 \(V \cup S\) 上有一阶连续偏导数，则有

\[\begin{align} \oint_{S}u\frac{\partial v}{\partial n}\mathrm{d}S = \iiint_{V}u\Delta v~\mathrm{d}V + \iiint_{V}\nabla u \cdot \nabla v~\mathrm{d}V \end{align}\]
\[\begin{align} \oint_{S}\Big( u\frac{\partial v}{\partial n} - v\frac{\partial u}{\partial n} \Big)~\mathrm{d}S = \iiint_{V}(u\Delta v - v\Delta u)\mathrm{d}V \end{align}\]

类似地，有二维Green公式

\[\begin{align} \oint_{l}u\frac{\partial v}{\partial n}\mathrm{d}l = \iint_{D}u\Delta v~\mathrm{d}A + \iint_{D}\nabla u \cdot \nabla v~\mathrm{d}A \end{align}\]
\[\begin{align} \oint_{l}\Big( u\frac{\partial v}{\partial n} - v\frac{\partial u}{\partial n} \Big)~\mathrm{d}l = \iint_{D}(u\Delta v - v\Delta u)\mathrm{d}A \end{align}\]

其中 \(l\) 是有界区域 \(D\) 的边界， \(\mathbf{n}\) 是边界的外法向。

可以得到一个推论，对于Helmholtz算子 \(L = \Delta \pm k^{2}\) ，也有Green第二公式。在二维情况时为

\[\begin{align} \oint_{l} \Big(u\frac{\partial v}{\partial n} - v \frac{\partial u}{\partial n}\Big)~\mathrm{d}l = \iint_{D}(u Lv - vLu)~\mathrm{d}A \end{align}\]

注解

求二维Helmholtz方程 \(\Delta_{2}u + cu = 0~(c = k^{2}>0)\) 的基本解，基本解满足方程

\[\begin{align} LU = \Delta_{2}U + k^{2}U = \delta(x,y) \end{align}\]

由方程的对称性，设 \(U = U(r)\) ，在极坐标下方程可以改写成

\[\begin{align} \frac{1}{r}\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}r}\Big(r\frac{\mathrm{d}U}{\mathrm{d}r}\Big) + k^{2}U = 0 ,\quad r > 0 \end{align}\]

也即

\[\begin{align} r^{2}U'' + rU' + k^{2}r^{2}U = 0 \end{align}\]

这是零阶Bessel方程，其通解为

\[\begin{align} U(r) = AJ_{0}(kr) + BN_{0}(kr) \end{align}\]

由于 \(J_{0}(kr)\) 在 \(r=0\) 无奇性，是齐次方程 \(\Delta_{2}u + k^{2}u = 0\) 在全平面的解，故可以取 \(A = 0\) 。而 \(N_{0}(kr)\) 在 \(r=0\) 有奇性，有望通过 \(B\) 的选取成为基本解。

令 \(U(r) = BN_{0}(kr) \sim B\frac{2}{\pi}\ln(kr)\) ，取 \(\varphi(x,y) \in C_{0}^{+\infty}(\mathbb{R}^{2})\) ，即在全平面上有任意阶连续偏导且在一个包含原点的有界区域 \(\Omega\) 外恒为零的函数（紧支函数），则

\[\begin{align} \varphi(0,0) = \iint_{\mathbb{R}^{2}}\delta(x,y)\varphi(x,y)~\mathrm{d}A = \iint_{\mathbb{R}^{2}}LU\varphi(x,y)~\mathrm{d}A = \iint_{\mathbb{R}^{2}}UL\varphi(x,y)~\mathrm{d}A \end{align}\]

上面的后一个等式来自广义函数求导的规定

\[\begin{align} \iint_{\mathbb{R}^{2}}\frac{\partial U}{\partial x}\varphi~\mathrm{d}A = -\iint_{\mathbb{R}^{2}}U\frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial x}~\mathrm{d}A ,\quad \iint_{\mathbb{R}^{2}}\frac{\partial U}{\partial y}\varphi~\mathrm{d}A = -\iint_{\mathbb{R}^{2}}U\frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial y}~\mathrm{d}A \end{align}\]

由于 \(U(r)\) 在 \(r = 0\) 有奇性，以原点为中心， \(\varepsilon\) 为半径取小圆盘 \(D_{\varepsilon}\) ，又由 \(\varphi(x,y)\) 的紧支性，不妨取包含原点的有界区域 \(D \supset \Omega\) ，则

\[\begin{align} \varphi(0,0) = \lim_{\varepsilon \to 0} \iint\limits_{D-D_{\varepsilon}}UL\varphi~\mathrm{d}A = \lim_{\varepsilon \to 0} \iint\limits_{D-D_{\varepsilon}}(U L\varphi - \varphi LU)~\mathrm{d}A \end{align}\]

由Green第二公式得到

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \varphi(0,0) &= \lim_{\varepsilon \to 0}\bigg[ \oint_{\partial D}\Big( U\frac{\partial\varphi}{\partial n} - \varphi\frac{\partial U}{\partial n} \Big)\mathrm{d}l - \oint_{\partial D_{\varepsilon}}\Big( U\frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial n} - \varphi\frac{\partial U}{\partial n} \Big)\mathrm{d}l \bigg] \\ &= \lim_{\varepsilon \to 0} \int_{\partial D_{\varepsilon}}\Big( \varphi\frac{\partial U}{\partial r} - U\frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial r} \Big)\mathrm{d}l \\ &= \lim_{\varepsilon \to 0} 2\pi \varepsilon \Big( \varphi \frac{\partial U}{\partial r} - U\frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial r} \Big)\Big|_{(x^{*},y^{*}) \in \partial D_{\varepsilon}} \\ &= \lim_{\varepsilon \to 0} 2\pi \varepsilon \Big[ \varphi(x^{*},y^{*})B\frac{2}{\pi\varepsilon} - B\frac{2}{\pi}\ln(k\varepsilon) \frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial r}(x^{*},y^{*}) \Big] \\ &= 4B \varphi(0,0) \end{align}\end{split}\]

所以 \(B = \frac{1}{4}\) ，得到二维Helmholtz方程 \(\Delta_{2}u + k^{2}u = 0\) 的基本解为

\[\begin{align} U(x,y) = \frac{1}{4}N_{0}(kr) \end{align}\]

注解

用同样的方法还可以求出二维Laplace方程 \(\Delta_{2}u = 0\) 的基本解

\[\begin{align} U(x,y) = -\frac{1}{2\pi}\ln\frac{1}{r} \end{align}\]

二维Helmholtz方程 \(\Delta_{2}u + cu = 0~(c = -k^{2} < 0)\) 的基本解

\[\begin{align} U(x,y) = -\frac{1}{2\pi}K_{0}(kr) \end{align}\]

三维Helmholtz方程 \(\Delta_{3}u + cu = 0\) 的基本解

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} U(x,y,z) = \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \frac{-e^{-\mathrm{i}kr}}{4\pi r} ~\text{or}~ -\frac{\cos kr}{4\pi r} ,\quad c=k^{2}>0 \\ -\frac{e^{-kr}}{4\pi r} ,\quad c = -k^{2}<0 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

边值问题的Green函数法¶

场位方程边值问题的Green函数及解的积分公式¶

首先讨论场位方程(Poisson方程)第一类边值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta u = - f(M) ,\quad M=(x,y,z)\in V, \\ u|_{\partial V} = \varphi(M) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

由叠加原理可知， \(u=u_{1}+u_{2}\) ， \(u_{1}\) 与 \(u_{2}\) 分别满足

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta u_{1} = - f(M) ,\quad M\in V, \\ u_{1}|_{\partial V} = 0 \end{array}\right. \qquad \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta u_{2} = 0 ,\quad M\in V, \\ u_{2}|_{\partial V} = \varphi(M) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

其中， \(u_{1}\) 表示在边界接地条件下体内电荷产生的电场， \(u_{2}\) 则为边界约束引起的电场。体内连续分布电荷 \(f(M)\) 可以表示成点源的叠加

\[\begin{align} f(M) = \int_{V} \delta(M-M_{0})f(M_{0})\mathrm{d}M_{0} \end{align}\]

注意到 \(u_{1}\) 的方程的边界条件是齐次的，只要求出点源 \(\delta(M-M_{0})\) 在齐次边界条件下的解，作相应的积分叠加，便可以得到连续源 \(f(M)\) 在齐次边界条件下的解。

我们称定解问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta G(M;M_{0}) = - \delta(M-M_{0}) ,\quad M,M_{0}\in V, \\ G|_{M\in\partial V} = 0 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

的解 \(G(M;M_{0})\) 为场为方程第一类边值问题式的Green函数。

注解

从物理上看，Green函数就是边界接地条件下，置于 \(V\) 内 \(M_{0}\) 点(源点)电荷为 \(+\varepsilon\) 的点源在 \(V\) 内 \(M\) 点(场点)产生的电场，仍然是一个点源函数，一个基本解。

由于边界的限制，它不能由原点的点源产生的场通过平移得到。这样，一个含有参数 \(M_{0}\) 的点源函数一般称之为Green函数。

为了由Green函数得到Poisson方程第一类边值问题的解，我们首先讨论Green函数的重要性质。

对称性： 设 \(G(M;M_{0})\) 为场位方程第一类边值问题式的Green函数，则 \(\forall M_{1},M_{2} \in V\) ，有

\[\begin{align} G(M_{2};M_{1}) = G(M_{1};M_{2}) \end{align}\]

这个性质在物理上称为 倒易性 ，说明不管 \(V\) 是什么样的区域，Green函数中的场点和源点可以互换，即在边界接地条件下 \(M_{1}\) 点的源在 \(M_{2}\) 点产生的场等同于 \(M_{2}\) 点的源在 \(M_{1}\) 点产生的场。

注解

对称性的证明如下：由Green函数的定义， \(G(M;M_{1})\) 和 \(G(M;M_{2})\) 分别满足边值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta G(M;M_{1}) = - \delta(M-M_{1}) ,\quad M,M_{1}\in V, \\ G(M;M_{1})|_{M\in \partial V} = 0 \end{array}\right. \qquad \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta G(M;M_{2}) = - \delta(M-M_{2}) ,\quad M,M_{2}\in V, \\ G(M;M_{2})|_{M\in \partial V} = 0 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

利用Green第二公式，有

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} G(M_{2};M_{1}) - G(M_{1};M_{2}) &= \int_{V} G(M;M_{1})\delta(M - M_{2})\mathrm{d}M - \int_{V} G(M;M_{2})\delta(M-M_{1})\mathrm{d}M \\ &= - \int_{V}\Big[ G(M;M_{1})\Delta G(M;M_{2}) - G(M;M_{2})\Delta G(M;M_{1}) \Big] \\ &= -\oint_{\partial V} \Big[ G(M;M_{1})\frac{\partial G(M;M_{2})}{\partial n} - G(M;M_{2})\frac{\partial G(M;M_{1})}{\partial n} \Big]\mathrm{d}S \\ &= 0 \end{align}\end{split}\]

需要说明的是，上述证明并不严格，因为Green公式成立的条件在这里并不满足。严格的证明应该按照瑕积分处理，在奇点 \(M_{1}\) 和 \(M_{2}\) 处挖去半径为 \(\varepsilon\) 的小球后应用Green公式，再令 \(\varepsilon \to 0\) 取极限证明。

下面利用Green函数给出场位方程第一类边值问题的积分公式(Poisson公式)。设 \(G(M;M_{0})\) 是场位方程第一类边值问题式的Green函数，则由

\[\begin{align} \int_{V}(u\Delta G - G \Delta u)\mathrm{d}M = \oint_{\partial V} \Big( u\frac{\partial G}{\partial n} - G\frac{\partial u}{\partial n} \Big)\mathrm{d}S \end{align}\]

将 \(u\) 和 \(G\) 满足的方程和边界条件代入，有

\[\begin{align} \int_{V} \big( -u\delta(M-M_{0}) + Gf \big)\mathrm{d}M = \oint_{\partial V}\varphi \frac{\partial G}{\partial n}\mathrm{d}S \end{align}\]

从而得到

\[\begin{align} u(M_{0}) = \int_{V}f(M)G(M;M_{0})\mathrm{d}M - \int_{\partial V}\varphi\frac{\partial G}{\partial n}\mathrm{d}S \end{align}\]

由于对称性，最终得到场位方程第一类边值问题式解的积分公式

\[\begin{align} u(M) = \int_{V}f(M_{0})G(M;M_{0})\mathrm{d}M_{0} - \int_{\partial V}\varphi(M_{0})\frac{\partial G}{\partial n}\mathrm{d}S_{0} \end{align}\]

对于场位方程第二、三类边值问题，也可以类似讨论。若定义定解问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta G(M;M_{0}) = -\delta(M-M_{0}) ,\quad M,M_{0}\in V \\ \Big( \alpha G + \beta \cfrac{\partial G}{\partial n} \Big)\bigg|_{\partial V} = 0 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

的解 \(G(M;M_{0})\) 为第三类边界条件下的Green函数，则相应的边值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta u = -f(M) ,\quad M\in V \\ \Big( \alpha u + \beta \cfrac{\partial u}{\partial n} \Big)\bigg|_{\partial V} = \varphi(M) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

的解的积分公式为

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} u(M) &= \int_{V}f(M_{0})G\mathrm{d}M_{0} + \frac{1}{\beta}\oint_{\partial V}\varphi(M_{0})G\mathrm{d}S_{0} \\ &= \int_{V} f(M_{0})G\mathrm{d}M_{0} - \frac{1}{\alpha}\oint_{\partial V}\varphi(M_{0})\frac{\partial G}{\partial n_{0}}\mathrm{d}S_{0} \end{align}\end{split}\]

当 \(\beta = 0\) 时即为第一类边值问题。当 \(\alpha = 0\) 时对应于第二类边值问题，但是此时前面定义的Green函数不存在。从物理上看，上面定义的Green函数表示内部有热源二边界绝热的稳恒温度场，这是不可能的。因此需要引进推广的Green函数

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta G = -\delta(M-M_{0}) + \frac{1}{v} ,\quad M,M_{0}\in V \\ \cfrac{\partial G}{\partial n}\bigg|_{\partial V} = 0 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

其中 \(v\) 是区域 \(V\) 的体积。相应边值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta u = -f(M) ,\quad M\in V \\ \cfrac{\partial u}{\partial n}\bigg|_{\partial V} = \varphi(M) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

当且仅当 \(\int_{V}f\mathrm{d}M = -\int_{\partial V}\varphi\mathrm{d}S\) 时，解的积分公式为

\[\begin{align} u(M) = \int_{V}f(M_{0})G\mathrm{d}M_{0} + \oint_{\partial V}\varphi(M_{0})G\mathrm{d}S_{0} + C \end{align}\]

以上Green函数的定义和解的积分公式在二维时同样适用，只需要将有关的体积分和边界曲面积分相应地改为平面区域 \(D\) 上的二重积分和边界曲线 \(\partial D\) 上的曲线积分。

Green函数的求法¶

场位方程边值问题的Green函数是含有广义函数 \(\delta(M-M_{0})\) 的特殊边值问题式的解。由于 \(\delta(M-M_{0})\) 可以像经典函数一样作Fourier展开和Fourier变换，因此Fourier方法是求Green函数的基本方法。对于某些特殊的区域和边界条件，则可以采用一些特殊方法求解。以下讨论的Green函数，如果不加说明，都是指Poisson方程第一类边值问题的Green函数。

镜像法¶

场位方程第一类边值问题的Green函数是定解问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta G = -\delta(M-M_{0}) ,\quad M,M_{0}\in V \\ G|_{\partial V} = 0 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

的解 \(G(M;M_{0})\) 。由叠加原理可得

\[\begin{align} G(M;M_{0}) = U(M;M_{0}) + g(M;M_{0}) \end{align}\]

其中 \(U\) 满足方程

\[\begin{align} \Delta U(M;M_{0}) = -\delta(M-M_{0}) \end{align}\]

是 \(M_{0}\) 点的点电荷产生的场。 \(g(M;M_{0})\) 满足Dirichlet问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta g(M;M_{0}) = 0 ,\quad M,M_{0} \in V \\ g|_{\partial V} = -U(M;M_{0})|_{\partial V} \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

是 \(M_{0}\) 的点电荷在边界上的感应电荷产生的电场。利用Laplace方程的基本解，容易得知在二、三维情形分别有

\[\begin{align} U(M;M_{0}) = \frac{1}{2\pi}\ln\frac{1}{r(M,M_{0})} ,\quad r(M,M_{0}) = \sqrt{(x-\xi)^{2} + (y - \eta)^{2}} \end{align}\]
\[\begin{align} U(M;M_{0}) = \frac{1}{4\pi r(M,M_{0})} ,\quad r(M,M_{0}) = \sqrt{(x-\xi)^{2} + (y-\eta)^{2} + (z-\zeta)^{2}} \end{align}\]

由于区域 \(V\) 外的点源在 \(V\) 内产生的电场满足Laplace方程，可以将边界感应电荷产生的电场 \(g(M;M_{0})\) 视作区域外某些虚设电荷产生的等效电场，这就是镜像法。困难就在于域外虚设电荷的电场与域内点电荷的电场在边界上必须相抵消，对于某些特殊区域 \(V\) ，这样的虚设电荷可以用初等方法找到。

注解

求上半空间( \(z > 0\) )Poisson方程第一类边值问题的Green函数。也就要解定解问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta G = -\delta(M - M_{0}) ,\quad z,\zeta >0 \\ G|_{z=0} = 0 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

\(M_{0}\) 点的正电荷 \(\varepsilon\) 在空间产生的电场为

\[\begin{align} U_{0} = \frac{1}{4\pi r(M,M_{0})} ,\quad r(M,M_{0}) = \sqrt{(x-\xi)^{2} + (y-\eta)^{2} + (z-\zeta)^{2}} \end{align}\]

边界面上 \(U_{0}|_{z=0} = \frac{1}{4\pi \sqrt{(x-\xi)^{2} + (y-\eta)^{2} + \zeta^{2}}}\) 。虚设电荷应该置于下半空间 \(M_{0}\) 关于平面 \(z=0\) 的对称点 \(M_{1}=(\xi,\eta,-\zeta)\) 上，电荷量为 \(-\varepsilon\) ，则该虚设电荷在空间产生的电场为

\[\begin{align} U_{1} = -\frac{1}{4\pi r(M,M_{1})} ,\quad r(M,M_{1}) = \sqrt{(x-\xi)^{2} + (y-\eta)^{2} + (z+\zeta)^{2}} \end{align}\]

在边界面上

\[\begin{align} U_{1}|_{z=0} = -\frac{1}{4\pi\sqrt{(x-\xi)^{2} + (y-\eta)^{2} + \zeta^{2}}} = -U_{0}|_{z=0} \end{align}\]

所以上半空间Poisson方程第一类边值问题的Green函数为

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} G(M;M_{0}) &= \frac{1}{4\pi r(M,M_{0})} - \frac{1}{4\pi r(M,M_{1})} \\ &= \frac{1}{4\pi}\Big[ \frac{1}{\sqrt{(x-\xi)^{2} + (y-\eta)^{2} + (z-\zeta)^{2}}} - \frac{1}{\sqrt{(x-\xi)^{2} + (y-\eta)^{2} + (z+\zeta)^{2}}} \Big] ,\quad z,\zeta > 0 \end{align}\end{split}\]

得到上述Green函数后，就有

\[\begin{align} \frac{\partial G}{\partial n}\Big|_{z=0} = - \frac{\partial G}{\partial z}\Big|_{z=0} = -\frac{\zeta}{2\pi \big((x-\xi)^{2} + (y-\eta)^{2} + \zeta^{2}\big)^{3/2}} \end{align}\]

从而可以得到Dirichlet问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta_{3}u = 0 ,\quad z>0 \\ u|_{z=0} = \varphi(x,y) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

的解的Poisson积分公式

\[\begin{align} u(\xi,\eta,\zeta) = \frac{1}{2\pi} \iint\limits_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\frac{\zeta \varphi(x,y)}{\big( (x-\xi)^{2} + (y-\eta)^{2} + \zeta^{2} \big)^{3/2}}\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y \end{align}\]

或者

\[\begin{align} u(x,y,z) = \frac{1}{2\pi} \iint\limits_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\frac{z \varphi(\xi,\eta)}{\big( (x-\xi)^{2} + (y-\eta)^{2} + z^{2} \big)^{3/2}}\mathrm{d}\xi\mathrm{d}\eta \end{align}\]

注解

在二维情形，若求上半平面Poisson方程第一类边值问题的Green函数，利用基本解 \(U = \frac{1}{2\pi}\ln r\) ，将虚设点电荷置于 \(M_{0}(\xi,\eta)\) 在下半平面的对称点 \(M_{1}(\xi,-\eta)\) 上，有

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} G(M;M_{0}) &= \frac{1}{2\pi}\Big[ \ln\frac{1}{r(M,M_{0})} - \ln\frac{1}{r(M,M_{1})}\Big] \\ &= \frac{1}{4\pi}\ln\frac{(x-\xi)^{2} + (y+\eta)^{2}}{(x-\xi)^{2} + (y-\eta)^{2}} ,\quad y,\eta > 0 \end{align}\end{split}\]

得到上述Green函数后，就可以得到上半平面Dirichlet问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta_{2}u = 0 ,\quad y>0 \\ u|_{y=0} = \varphi(x) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

的解的积分公式为

\[\begin{align} u(x,y) = \frac{1}{\pi}\int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\frac{y\varphi(\xi)}{(x-\xi)^{2} + y^{2}}\mathrm{d}\xi \end{align}\]

注解

求半径为 \(R\) 的球域内Poisson方程第一类边值问题的Green函数。球域内Green函数的定解问题为

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta_{3}G = -\delta(M-M_{0}) ,\quad 0\le r, \rho <R \\ G|_{r=R} = 0 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

其中 \(r=\sqrt{x^{2}+y^{2}+z^{2}}, \rho=\sqrt{\xi^{2}+\eta^{2}+\zeta^{2}}\) 。球内 \(M_{0}\) 点正电荷 \(\varepsilon\) 在 \(M\) 点的电场为 \(U_{0} = \frac{1}{4\pi r(M,M_{0})}\) 。该电场关于射线 \(OM_{0}\) 轴对称，虚设电荷 \(-Q\) 应该置于球外 \(OM_{0}\) 射线的某一点 \(M_{1}\) 上。虚设电荷与 \(M_{0}\) 点真实点电荷在球面上产生的电位要相抵消，即对于球面上任一点 \(M\) ，有

\[\begin{align} U_{0} + U_{1} = \frac{1}{4\pi r(M,M_{0})} - \frac{Q/\varepsilon}{4\pi r(M,M_{1})} = 0 \end{align}\]

因此， \(M_{1}\) 需要满足

\[\begin{align} \frac{r(M,M_{1})}{r(M,M_{0})} = \frac{Q}{\varepsilon} \end{align}\]

由几何知识可知，取 \(M_{1}\) 为 \(M_{0}\) 关于球面的对称点时( \(r(O,M_{0})\cdot r(O,M_{1}) = R^{2}\) )，三角形 \(OM_{0}M\) 与三角形 \(OMM_{1}\) 相似，从而有

\[\begin{align} \frac{r(M,M_{1})}{r(M,M_{0})} = \frac{r(O,M)}{r(O,M_{0})} = \frac{R}{\rho} \end{align}\]

故虚设电荷应该置于 \(M_{0}\) 关于球面的对称点 \(M_{1}\) 上，电荷量应该为 \(-Q = -\frac{R}{\rho}\varepsilon\) 。从而球内Green函数

\[\begin{align} G(M;M_{0}) = \frac{1}{4\pi}\Big[ \frac{1}{r(M,M_{0})} - \frac{R}{\rho r(M,M_{1})} \Big] \end{align}\]

取球坐标，记场点 \(M=(r,\theta,\varphi)\) ，源点 \(M_{0}=(\rho,\theta_{0},\varphi_{0})\) ， \(\psi\) 为 \(OM_{0}\) 与 \(OM\) 的夹角，则

\[\begin{align} r(M,M_{0}) = \sqrt{r^{2} + \rho^{2} - 2r\rho \cos\psi} \end{align}\]
\[\begin{align} r(M,M_{1}) = \sqrt{r^{2} + (\frac{R^{2}}{\rho})^{2} - 2r\frac{R^{2}}{\rho}\cos\psi} = \frac{1}{\rho}\sqrt{\rho^{2}r^{2} + R^{4} - 2\rho r R^{2}\cos\psi} \end{align}\]
\[\begin{align} \cos\psi = \cos\theta\cos\theta_{0} + \sin\theta\sin\theta_{0}\cos(\varphi-\varphi_{0}) \end{align}\]

从而有

\[\begin{align} G(M;M_{0}) = \frac{1}{4\pi}\bigg[ \frac{1}{\sqrt{r^{2} + \rho^{2} - 2\rho r \cos\psi}} - \frac{R}{\sqrt{\rho^{2}r^{2} + R^{4} - 2\rho r R^{2} \cos\psi}} \bigg] \end{align}\]

在得到上面这个Green函数之后，就可得知在球面上

\[\begin{align} \frac{\partial G}{\partial n}\Big|_{r=R} = \frac{\partial G}{\partial r}\Big|_{r=R} = -\frac{R^{2} - \rho^{2}}{4\pi R(R^{2} + \rho^{2} - 2\rho R\cos\psi)^{3/2}} \end{align}\]

进而可得Dirichlet问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta_{3}u = 0 ,\quad r<R \\ u|_{r=R} = f(\theta,\varphi) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

的解的Poisson积分公式

\[\begin{align} u(\rho,\theta_{0},\varphi_{0}) = \frac{1}{4\pi R}\oint_{S_{R}}\frac{R^{2} - \rho^{2}}{(R^{2} + \rho^{2} - 2R\rho\cos\psi)^{3/2}}f(\theta,\varphi)\mathrm{d}S \end{align}\]

或者

\[\begin{align} u(r,\theta,\varphi) = \frac{1}{4\pi R} \oint_{S_{R}}\frac{R^{2} - r^{2}}{(R^{2} + r^{2} - 2Rr\cos\psi)^{3/2}}f(\theta_{0},\varphi_{0})\mathrm{d}S_{0} \end{align}\]

其中 \(S_{R}\) 为以 \(O\) 为球心、 \(R\) 为半径的球面。如果取 \(M_{0}\) 为球心 \(O\) ， \(\rho = 0\) ，则上式变为

\[\begin{align} u(O) = \frac{1}{4\pi R^{2}}\oint_{S_{R}}f(M)\mathrm{d}S \end{align}\]

这说明Laplace方程的解在球心的值等于它的球面平均值。

注解

求圆域内Poisson方程第一类边值问题的Green函数。该Green函数满足

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta_{2}G = -\delta(M-M_{0}) ,\quad r=\sqrt{x^{2}+y^{2}}<R , \rho = \sqrt{\xi^{2} + \eta^{2}}<R \\ G|_{r=R} = 0 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

圆内过 \(M_{0}=(\xi,\eta)\) 点的线电荷 \(\varepsilon\) 在 \(M\) 点的电位为

\[\begin{align} U_{0} = \frac{1}{2\pi}\ln\frac{1}{r(M,M_{0})} \end{align}\]

在 \(M_{0}\) 点关于圆周的对称点 \(M_{1}\) 上放置虚设线电荷 \(-Q\) 产生的电位为

\[\begin{align} U_{1} = -\frac{Q}{2\pi \varepsilon}\ln\frac{1}{r(M,M_{1})} + C \end{align}\]

因为Laplace方程的基本解不唯一，这里添加了待定常数 \(C\) 。于是Green函数满足形式

\[\begin{align} G(M;M_{0}) = \frac{1}{2\pi}\bigg[ \ln\frac{1}{r(M,M_{0})} - \frac{Q}{\varepsilon}\ln\frac{1}{r(M,M_{1})}\bigg] + C \end{align}\]

当 \(M\) 在圆域边界上， \(r(M,M_{1}) = \frac{R}{\rho}r(M,M_{0})\) ，边界条件为

\[\begin{align} G|_{r=R} = \frac{1}{2\pi}\bigg[ \ln\frac{1}{r(M,M_{0})} - \frac{Q}{\varepsilon}\ln\frac{1}{r(M,M_{0})} - \frac{Q}{\varepsilon}\ln\frac{\rho}{R}\bigg] + C = 0 \end{align}\]

从中推出 \(Q = \varepsilon\) 和 \(C = -\frac{1}{2\pi}\ln\frac{R}{\rho}\) ，最终得到圆内Green函数

\[\begin{align} G(M;M_{0}) = \frac{1}{2\pi}\bigg[ \ln\frac{1}{r(M,M_{0})} - \ln\frac{R}{\rho r(M,M_{1})} \bigg] \end{align}\]

取极坐标 \(M=(r,\theta), M_{0}=(\rho,\theta_{0}), \psi=\theta - \theta_{0}\) ，有

\[\begin{align} G(M;M_{0}) = \frac{1}{4\pi}\ln \frac{R^{4} + r^{2}\rho^{2} - 2R^{2}r\rho\cos\psi}{R^{2}(r^{2} + \rho^{2} - 2r\rho\cos\psi)} \end{align}\]

得到上述Green函数后，则有

\[\begin{align} \frac{\partial G}{\partial n}\Big|_{r=R} = \frac{\partial G}{\partial r}\Big|_{r=R} = -\frac{1}{2\pi}\frac{R^{2} - \rho^{2}}{R(R^{2} + \rho^{2} - 2R\rho\cos\psi)} \end{align}\]

从而可知圆内Laplace方程的Dirichlet问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta_{2}u = 0 ,\quad r<R \\ u|_{r=R} = \varphi(\theta) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

的解可以表示为Poisson积分公式

\[\begin{align} u(M_{0}) = u(\rho,\theta_{0}) = \frac{1}{2\pi}\int_{0}^{2\pi}\frac{(R^{2} - \rho^{2})\varphi(\theta)}{R^{2} + \rho^{2} - 2R\rho\cos(\theta - \theta_{0})}\mathrm{d}\theta \end{align}\]

或者

\[\begin{align} u(M) = u(r,\theta) = \frac{1}{2\pi}\int_{0}^{2\pi}\frac{(R^{2} - r^{2})\varphi(\theta_{0})}{R^{2} + r^{2} - 2Rr\cos(\theta - \theta_{0})}\mathrm{d}\theta_{0} \end{align}\]

注解

第一象限内场位方程第一边值问题的Green函数为

\[\begin{align} G(M;M_{0}) = \frac{1}{2\pi}\bigg[ \ln\frac{1}{r(M,M_{0})} - \ln\frac{1}{r(M,M_{1})} - \ln\frac{1}{r(M,M_{2})} + \ln\frac{1}{r(M,M_{3})} \bigg] \end{align}\]

其中， \(M_{0}=(\xi,\eta)\) 是真实源点， \(M_{1}=(\xi,-\eta), M_{2}=(-\xi,\eta),M_{3}=(-\xi,-\eta)\) 为虚设电荷点，分别是 \(M_{0}\) 关于 \(x\) 轴、 \(y\) 轴和原点的对称点。

Fourier方法¶

Fourier方法是指按照固有函数作广义Fourier展开的方法，包括分离变量和积分变换，仍然是求Green函数的基本方法。

注解

半径为 \(R\) 的匀质球内， \(M_{0}\) 点处有强度为 \(Q\) 的热源，球面与温度为零摄氏度的外界自由热交换，求达到稳恒后球内的温度分布。

这是点源引起的温度分布，稳恒温度 \(u(x,y,z)\) 满足

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta_{3}u = -\cfrac{Q}{k}\delta(M-M_{0}) ,\quad r,\rho<R \\ \Big( k\cfrac{\partial u}{\partial r} + hu \Big)\Big|_{r=R} = 0 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

其中 \(k\) 为介质内热传导系数， \(h\) 为边界面热交换系数。如果取 \(Q=k\) ，那么 \(u\) 即为Poisson方程第三类边界条件的Green函数。

由Laplace方程的基本解，令 \(U(M;M_{0}) = \frac{1}{4\pi r(M,M_{0})}\) ，则

\[\begin{align} u(M;M_{0}) = \frac{Q}{k}U(M;M_{0}) + g(M;M_{0}) \end{align}\]

则 \(g(M;M_{0})\) 满足

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta_{3}g = 0 ,\quad r<R \\ \Big(k\cfrac{\partial g}{\partial r} + hg\Big)\Big|_{r=R} = -\cfrac{Q}{k}\Big( k\cfrac{\partial U}{\partial r}+hU \Big)\Big|_{r=R} \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

由于温度分布关于球心到 \(M_{0}\) 点的 \(OM_{0}\) 轴对称，将 \(OM_{0}\) 轴取作极轴，由球内Laplace方程解的一般形式式可知

\[\begin{align} g(M;M_{0}) = \sum_{n=0}^{+\infty}C_{n}\Big(\frac{r}{R}\Big)^{n}P_{n}(\cos\theta) \end{align}\]

进而

\[\begin{align} \Big( k\cfrac{\partial g}{\partial r} + hg \Big)\Big|_{r=R} = \sum_{n=0}^{+\infty}\Big( \frac{nk}{R} + h \Big)C_{n}P_{n}(\cos\theta) \end{align}\]

利用Legendre多项式的母函数式，当 \(\rho < r\) 时，有

\[\begin{align} \frac{1}{r(M,M_{0})} = \frac{1}{(r^{2} + \rho^{2} - 2r\rho \cos\theta)^{1/2}} = \frac{1}{r}\sum_{n=0}^{+\infty}\Big(\frac{\rho}{r}\Big)^{n}P_{n}(\cos\theta) \end{align}\]

所以

\[\begin{align} -\frac{Q}{k}\Big( k\frac{\partial U}{\partial r} + hU \Big)\Big|_{r=R} = -\frac{Q}{k}\sum_{n=0}^{+\infty}\frac{hR - (n+1)k}{4\pi R^{n+2}}\rho^{n}P_{n}(\cos\theta) \end{align}\]

代入边界条件，比较系数，解得

\[\begin{align} C_{n} = \frac{Q}{k}\frac{(n+1)k - hR}{hR + nk}\cdot \frac{\rho^{n}}{4\pi R^{n+1}} \end{align}\]

故温度分布为

\[\begin{align} u = \frac{Q}{4\pi k}\bigg[ \frac{1}{r(M,M_{0})} + \sum_{n=0}^{+\infty}\frac{(n+1)k - hR}{(hR + nk)R}\Big(\frac{\rho r}{R^{2}}\Big)^{n}P_{n}(\cos\theta) \bigg] \end{align}\]

当 \(\rho > r\) 时该式仍然成立。

注解

求矩形域 \(D: 0<x<a, 0<y<b\) 内Poisson方程第一类边值问题的Green函数。也即求解边值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta_{2}G = -\delta(x-\xi, y-\eta) ,\quad 0<x,\xi<a, 0<y,\eta<b \\ G|_{x=0} = G|_{x=a} = G|_{y=0} = G|_{y=b} = 0 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

考虑同一齐次边界条件下Laplace算子的固有值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta_{2}v + \lambda v = 0 ,\quad 0<x<a, 0<y<b \\ v|_{x=0} = v|_{x=a} = v|_{y=0} = v|_{y=b} = 0 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

令 \(v(x,y) = X(x)Y(y)\) ，分离得到常微分方程的固有值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} X'' + \mu X = 0 ,\quad 0<x<a \\ X(0) = X(a) = 0 \end{array}\right. \qquad \left\{\begin{array}{l} Y'' + \nu Y = 0 ,\quad 0<y<b \\ Y(0) = Y(b) = 0 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

且 \(\mu + \nu = \lambda\) 。解得固有值和固有函数分别为

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} & \mu_{n} = \Big(\frac{n\pi}{a}\Big)^{2} ,\quad X_{n}(x) = \sin\frac{n\pi}{a}x ,\quad n=1,2,\cdots \\ & \nu_{m} = \Big(\frac{m\pi}{b}\Big)^{2} ,\quad Y_{m}(y) = \sin\frac{m\pi}{b}y ,\quad m=1,2,\cdots \end{align}\end{split}\]

所以相应的Laplace方程的固有值问题有固有值和固有函数

\[\begin{align} \lambda_{nm} = \Big(\frac{n\pi}{a}\Big)^{2} + \Big(\frac{m\pi}{b}\Big)^{2} \end{align}\]
\[\begin{align} v_{nm}(x,y) = \sin\frac{n\pi}{a}x\sin\frac{m\pi}{b}y ,\quad n,m=1,2,\cdots \end{align}\]

由于 \(\left \{ v_{nm}(x,y) \right \}~(n,m=1,2,\cdots)\) 是该矩形区域上的完备正交函数系，设Green函数

\[\begin{align} G = \sum_{n,m=1}^{+\infty}C_{nm}v_{nm}(x,y) \end{align}\]

则有

\[\begin{align} \Delta_{2}G = -\sum_{n,m=1}^{+\infty}C_{nm}\Big[\Big(\frac{n\pi}{a}\Big)^{2} + \Big(\frac{m\pi}{b}\Big)^{2}\Big]v_{nm}(x,y) \end{align}\]

又因为

\[\begin{align} \delta(x-\xi, y-\eta) = \sum_{n,m=1}^{+\infty}B_{nm}v_{nm}(x,y) \end{align}\]
\[\begin{align} B_{nm} = \frac{1}{\| v_{nm}(x,y) \|^{2}}\int_{0}^{a}\int_{0}^{b}\delta(x-\xi,y-\eta)\sin\frac{n\pi}{a}x\sin\frac{m\pi}{b}y\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y = \frac{4}{ab}\sin\frac{n\pi}{a}\xi \sin\frac{m\pi}{b}\eta \end{align}\]

代入 \(G\) 的方程，两边比较系数，确定

\[\begin{align} C_{nm} = \frac{4}{ab}\Big[ \Big(\frac{n\pi}{a}\Big)^{2} + \Big(\frac{m\pi}{b}\Big)^{2} \Big]^{-1} \sin\frac{n\pi}{a}\xi \sin\frac{m\pi}{b}\eta \end{align}\]

得到矩形域上Dirichlet问题的Green函数

\[\begin{align} G(x,y;\xi,\eta) = \frac{4ab}{\pi^{2}}\sum_{n=1}^{+\infty}\sum_{m=1}^{+\infty} \frac{1}{(nb)^{2} + (ma)^{2}} \sin\frac{n\pi}{a}\xi \sin\frac{m\pi}{b}\eta \sin\frac{n\pi}{a}x \sin\frac{m\pi}{b}y \end{align}\]

注解

求半条形区域 \(D: 0<x<a, y>0\) 内Poisson方程第一类边值问题的Green函数。即解定解问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta_{2}G = -\delta(x-\xi, y-\eta) ,\quad 0<x,\xi<a, \quad y,\eta >0 \\ G|_{x=0} = G|_{x=a} = G|_{y=0} = 0 \\ G|_{y\to +\infty}\text{有界} \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

考虑相应偏微分方程固有值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta_{2}v + \lambda v = 0 ,\quad 0<x<a,~ y>0 \\ v|_{x=0} = v|_{x=a} = v|_{y=0} = 0 \\ v|_{y\to\infty}\text{有界} \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

令 \(v=X(x)Y(y)\) ，分离出两个常微分方程固有值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} X'' + \mu X = 0 ,\quad 0<x<a \\ X(0) = X(a) = 0 \end{array}\right. \qquad \left\{\begin{array}{l} Y'' + \nu Y = 0 ,\quad 0<y<+\infty \\ Y(0) = 0 ,\quad Y(+\infty)\text{有界} \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

其中 \(\mu + \nu = \lambda\) 。分别解得

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} & \mu_{n} = \Big(\frac{n\pi}{a}\Big)^{2} ,\quad X_{n}(x) = \sin\frac{n\pi}{a}x ,\quad n=1,2,\cdots \\ & \nu = \omega^{2} ,\quad Y(y,\omega) = \sin \omega y ,\quad \omega >0 \end{align}\end{split}\]

故相应偏微分方程固有值问题有固有值和固有函数系

\[\begin{align} \lambda_{n\omega} = \Big(\frac{n\pi}{a}\Big)^{2} + \omega^{2} ,\quad v_{n}(x,y,\omega) = \sin\frac{n\pi}{a}x\sin\omega y \end{align}\]

设 \(G\) 满足形式

\[\begin{align} G = \sum\limits_{n=1}^{+\infty}\int_{0}^{+\infty}C_{n}(\omega)\sin\omega y \mathrm{d}\omega \sin\frac{n\pi}{a}x \end{align}\]

代入 \(G\) 的方程得到

\[\begin{align} -\Delta_{2}G = \sum_{n=1}^{+\infty}\bigg[ \int_{0}^{+\infty}C_{n}(\omega)\Big((\frac{n\pi}{a})^{2} + \omega^{2}\Big)\sin \omega y \mathrm{d}\omega \bigg] \sin\frac{n\pi}{a}x = \delta(x-\xi,y-\eta) \end{align}\]

上式可以看成是 \(C_{n}(\omega)\Big((\frac{n\pi}{a})^{2} + \omega^{2}\Big)\) 的正弦变换，由反变换公式求出

\[\begin{align} C_{n}(\omega)\Big((\frac{n\pi}{a})^{2} + \omega^{2}\Big) = \frac{2}{\pi}\int_{0}^{+\infty}\Big[ \frac{2}{a}\sin\frac{n\pi}{a}\xi \delta(y-\eta) \Big]\sin\omega y \mathrm{d}y = \frac{4}{a\pi}\sin\frac{n\pi}{a}\xi \sin\omega \eta \end{align}\]

因此

\[\begin{align} C_{n}(\omega) = \frac{4a}{\pi [(n\pi)^{2} + (a\omega)^{2}]}\sin\frac{n\pi}{a}\xi \sin \omega \eta \end{align}\]

所以Green函数

\[\begin{align} G(x,y;\xi,\eta) = \frac{4a}{\pi}\sum_{n=1}^{+\infty}\Big[ \int_{0}^{+\infty}\frac{\sin\omega\eta \sin\omega y}{(n\pi)^{2} + (a\omega)^{2}}\mathrm{d}\omega \Big] \sin\frac{n\pi}{a}\xi \sin\frac{n\pi}{a}x \end{align}\]

Helmholtz方程边值问题及其Green函数¶

Helmholtz方程第一类边值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta_{3}u + k^{2}u = f(M) ,\quad M=(x,y,z) \in V \\ u|_{\partial V} = \varphi(M)|_{\partial V} \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

当 \(k^{2}\) 不是固有值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta_{3}v + \lambda v = 0 ,\quad M\in V \\ v|_{\partial V} = 0 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

的固有值时，问题式的解存在且唯一。

如果 \(G(M;M_{0})\) 满足

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \Delta_{3}G + k^{2}G = \delta(M-M_{0}) ,\quad M,M_{0} \in V \\ G|_{\partial V} = 0 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

则称 \(G(M;M_{0})\) 为Helmholtz方程第一类边值问题的Green函数。

由Helmholtz算子 \(L = \Delta + k^{2}\) 的Green第二公式，同样可以证明 \(G(M;M_{0}) = G(M_{0};M)\) ，且有问题式解的积分公式：如果 \(G(M;M_{0})\) 是Helmholtz方程第一类边值问题的Green函数，则问题式的解为

\[\begin{align} u(M_{0}) = \int_{V}f(M)G(M;M_{0})\mathrm{d}M + \oint_{\partial V}\varphi(M)\frac{\partial G}{\partial n}\mathrm{d}S \end{align}\]

或者

\[\begin{align} u(M) = \int_{V} f(M_{0})G(M;M_{0})\mathrm{d}M_{0} + \oint_{\partial V}\varphi(M_{0})\frac{\partial G}{\partial n}\mathrm{d}S_{0} \end{align}\]

求Green函数的基本方法是广义Fourier展开。如果已知固有值问题式的固有值 \(\{ \lambda_{nml} \}\) ，固有函数 \(\{ v_{nml}(M) \}\) ，它们构成区域 \(V\) 上的完备正交函数系，从而可以设

\[\begin{align} G(M;M_{0}) = \sum_{n,m,l}C_{nml}v_{nml}(M) \end{align}\]

代入方程确定 \(C_{nml}\) ，最后得到

\[\begin{align} G(M;M_{0}) = \sum_{n,m,l}\frac{1}{(k^{2} - \lambda_{nml})\| v_{nml}(M) \|^{2}}v_{nml}(M_{0})v_{nml}(M) \end{align}\]

当 \(V\) 为某些特殊区域时，也可以用镜像法求Green函数。

初值问题的基本解方法¶

ut=Lu型方程初值问题的基本解¶

考虑初值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \cfrac{\partial u}{\partial t} = Lu + f(t,M) ,\quad t>0, M\in \mathbb{R}^{n}, n=1,2,3 \\ u|_{t=0} = \varphi(M) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

其中 \(L\) 是关于空间变量 \(M\) 的常系数线性偏微分算子。一般地，我们定义下列初值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \cfrac{\partial U}{\partial t} = LU ,\quad t>0, M\in\mathbb{R}^{n}, n=1,2,3 \\ U|_{t=0} = \delta(M) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

的解 \(U(t,M)\) 为方程 \(\frac{\partial u}{\partial t} = Lu\) 的初值问题式的基本解，而在得到该基本解后，就可以得到原初值问题的解为

\[\begin{align} u(t,M) = U(t,M) * \varphi(M) + \int_{0}^{t}U(t-\tau, M) * f(\tau, M)~\mathrm{d}\tau \end{align}\]

注解

上述解的积分公式的证明如下：令 \(u_{1} = U(t,M) * \varphi(M)\) ， \(u_{2} = \int_{0}^{t}U(t-\tau,M)*f(\tau,M)\mathrm{d}\tau\) 。根据基本解的定义，容易直接验证

\[\begin{align} \frac{\partial u_{1}}{\partial t} = \frac{\partial }{\partial t}[U(t,M)*\varphi(M)] = \Big[ \frac{\partial }{\partial t}U(t,M) \Big] * \varphi(M) = [LU(t,M)]*\varphi(M) = L[U(t,M) * \varphi(M)] = Lu_{1} \end{align}\]
\[\begin{align} u_{1}|_{t=0} = [U(t,M) * \varphi(M)]\Big|_{t=0} = U(t,M) \Big|_{t=0} * \varphi(M) = \delta(M) * \varphi(M) = \varphi(M) \end{align}\]
\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \frac{\partial u_{2}}{\partial t} &= \frac{\partial }{\partial t} \int_{0}^{t} U(t-\tau, M) * f(\tau,M)\mathrm{d}\tau \\ &= \int_{0}^{t} \frac{\partial }{\partial t}U(t-\tau,M) * f(\tau,M)\mathrm{d}\tau + U(0,M) * f(t,M) \\ &= \int_{0}^{t} LU(t-\tau, M) * f(\tau,M)\mathrm{d}\tau + \delta(M) * f(t,M) \\ &= \int_{0}^{t} L[U(t-\tau,M) * f(\tau,M)]\mathrm{d}\tau + f(t,M) \\ & = Lu_{2} + f(t,M) \end{align}\end{split}\]
\[\begin{align} u_{2}|_{t=0} = 0 \end{align}\]

再由叠加原理可知 \(u = u_{1} + u_{2}\) 满足初值问题式。

这里我们反复交换积分与求导，积分与取极限的次序，从广义函数来看，都是允许的。

utt=Lu型方程问题的基本解¶

考虑初值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \cfrac{\partial^{2}u}{\partial t^{2}} = Lu + f(t,M) ,\quad t>0, M\in \mathbb{R}^{n}, n=1,2,3 \\ u|_{t=0} = \varphi(M), \quad \cfrac{\partial u}{\partial t}\Big|_{t=0} = \psi(M) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

其中 \(L\) 是关于空间变量 \(M\) 的常系数线性偏微分算子。我们定义下列初值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \cfrac{\partial^{2}U}{\partial t^{2}} = LU,\quad t>0, M\in \mathbb{R}^{n}, n=1,2,3 \\ U|_{t=0} = 0, \quad \cfrac{\partial U}{\partial t}\Big|_{t=0} = \delta(M) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

的解 \(U(t,M)\) 为方程 \(\frac{\partial^{2}u}{\partial t^{2}} = Lu\) 的初值问题式的基本解。在得知该基本解后，则原初值问题的解为

\[\begin{align} u(t,M) = U(t,M) * \psi(M) + \frac{\partial }{\partial t}[U(t,M) * \varphi(M)] + \int_{0}^{t} U(t-\tau, M) * f(\tau,M)\mathrm{d}\tau \end{align}\]

热传导方程的初值问题¶

考虑 \(n\) 维热传导方程初值问题的基本解，即求解初值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \cfrac{\partial}{\partial t}U = a^{2}\Delta_{n}U ,\quad t>0, \mathbf{x}=(x_{1},x_{2},\cdots,x_{n})\in\mathbb{R}^{n} \\ U|_{t=0} = \delta(\mathbf{x}) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

采用Fourier变换进行处理，对上式作 \(n\) 维FT，记 \(\hat{U}(t,\boldsymbol{\lambda}) = F[U(t,\mathbf{x})], \boldsymbol{\lambda}=(\lambda_{1},\lambda_{2},\cdots,\lambda_{n})\in\mathbb{R}^{n}\) ，得到

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \cfrac{\mathrm{d}\hat{U}}{\mathrm{d}t} = -a^{2}\rho^{2}\hat{U} ,\quad \rho^{2} = \sum\limits_{j=1}^{n}\lambda_{j}^{2} \\ \hat{U}|_{t=0} = 1 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

可知，像函数为

\[\begin{align} \hat{U}(t,\boldsymbol{\lambda}) = e^{-a^{2}\rho^{2}t} \end{align}\]

对像函数作反变换，求得基本解为

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} U(t,\mathbf{x}) &= \frac{1}{(2\pi)^{n}}\int_{\mathbb{R}^{n}}e^{-a^{2}\rho^{2}t}\cdot e^{-\boldsymbol{\lambda}\cdot \mathbf{x}}\mathrm{d}\boldsymbol{\lambda} \\ &= \prod_{j=1}^{n} \Big[ \frac{1}{2\pi}\int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}e^{-a^{2}\lambda_{j}^{2}t} \cdot e^{\mathrm{i}\lambda_{j}x_{j}}\mathrm{d}\lambda_{j} \Big] \\ &= \prod_{j=1}^{n} \frac{1}{2a\sqrt{\pi t}}e^{-\cfrac{x_{j}^{2}}{4a^{2}t}} \\ &= \Big( \frac{1}{2a\sqrt{\pi t}} \Big)^{n} e^{-\cfrac{x_{1}^{2} + x_{2}^{2} + \cdots + x_{n}^{2}}{4a^{2}t}} \end{align}\end{split}\]

根据这个基本解，我们可以得知热传导方程初值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \cfrac{\partial u}{\partial t} = a^{2}\Delta_{n}u + f(t,\mathbf{x}) ,\quad t>0, \mathbf{x}\in\mathbb{R}^{n} \\ u|_{t=0} = \varphi(\mathbf{x}) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

的解为

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} u(t,\mathbf{x}) &= U(t,\mathbf{x}) * \varphi(\mathbf{x}) + \int_{0}^{t}U(t-\tau, \mathbf{x}) * f(\tau,\mathbf{x})\mathrm{d}\tau \\ &= \Big( \frac{1}{2a\sqrt{\pi t}} \Big)^{n} \int_{\mathbb{R}^{n}} \varphi(\mathbf{x}') \exp\Big( -\frac{|\mathbf{x} - \mathbf{x}'|}{4a^{2}t} \Big)\mathrm{d}\mathbf{x}' \\ &\quad + \Big( \frac{1}{2a\sqrt{\pi t}} \Big)^{n} \int_{0}^{t} \frac{\mathrm{d}\tau}{(\sqrt{t-\tau})^{n}} \int_{\mathbb{R}^{n}} f(\tau, \mathbf{x}') \exp\Big( -\frac{|\mathbf{x} - \mathbf{x}'|}{4a^{2}(t-\tau)} \Big)\mathrm{d}\mathbf{x}' \end{align}\end{split}\]

其中，积分变量 \(\mathbf{x}' = (\xi_{1}, \xi_{2}, \cdots, \xi_{n}) \in \mathbb{R}^{n}\) 。

波动方程的初值问题¶

考虑单波方程初值问题的基本解，也即求解初值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \cfrac{\partial U}{\partial t} + a\cfrac{\partial U}{\partial x} = 0 ,\quad t>0, -\infty<x<+\infty \\ U|_{t=0} = \delta(x) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

对上述方程和初始条件作Fourier变换，记 \(\hat{U}(t,\lambda) = F[U(t,x)]\) ，得到

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \cfrac{\mathrm{d}\hat{U}}{\mathrm{d}t} + \mathrm{i}a\lambda\hat{U} = 0 \\ \hat{U}|_{t=0} = 1 \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

此常微分方程初值问题的解

\[\begin{align} \hat{U}(t,x) = e^{-\mathrm{i}a\lambda t} \end{align}\]

作反变换，得到

\[\begin{align} U(t,x) = F^{-1}[e^{-\mathrm{i}a\lambda t}] = \delta(x-at) \end{align}\]

根据该基本解，可以直接得到单波方程初值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \cfrac{\partial u}{\partial t} + a\cfrac{\partial u}{\partial x} = f(t,x) ,\quad t>0, -\infty<x<+\infty \\ u|_{t=0} = \varphi(x) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

的解为

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} u(t,x) &= \delta(x-at) * \varphi(x) + \int_{0}^{t} \delta\big(x-a(t-\tau)\big) * f(\tau,x)\mathrm{d}\tau \\ &= \varphi(x-at) + \int_{0}^{t} f\big(\tau, x-a(t-\tau)\big)\mathrm{d}\tau \\ &= \varphi(x-at) + \frac{1}{a}\int_{x-at}^{x} f\Big(t-\frac{x-\xi}{a}, \xi\Big)\mathrm{d}\xi \end{align}\end{split}\]

考虑三维波动方程初值问题的基本解，也就是求解初值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{\begin{array}{l} \cfrac{\partial^{2}U}{\partial t^{2}} = a^{2}\Delta_{3}U ,\quad t>0, -\infty<x,y,z<+\infty \\ U|_{t=0} = 0,\quad \cfrac{\partial U}{\partial t}\Big|_{t=0} = \delta(x,y,z) \end{array}\right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

对方程和初始条件作Fourier变换，记 \(\hat{U}(t,\lambda,\mu,\nu) = F[U(t,x,y,z)]\) ，得到常微分方程初值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \cfrac{\mathrm{d}^{2}\hat{U}}{\mathrm{d}t^{t}} = -a^{2}\rho^{2}\hat{U} ,\quad t>0, -\infty<\lambda,\mu,\nu<+\infty \\ \hat{U}|_{t=0} = 0 ,\quad \cfrac{\partial \hat{U}}{\partial t}\Big|_{t=0} = 1 \end{array} \right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

其中 \(\rho = \sqrt{\lambda^{2} + \mu^{2} + \nu^{2}}\) 。该初值问题的解为

\[\begin{align} \hat{U}(t,\lambda,\mu,\nu) = \frac{\sin a\rho t}{a\rho} \end{align}\]

作反变换，得到

\[\begin{align} U(t,x,y,z) = \frac{1}{(2\pi)^{3}} \iiint\limits_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\frac{\sin a\rho t}{a\rho} e^{\mathrm{i}(\lambda x + \mu y + \nu z)}\mathrm{d}\lambda\mathrm{d}\mu\mathrm{d}\nu = \frac{1}{(2\pi)^{3}} \iiint\limits_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\frac{\sin a\rho t}{a\rho} e^{\mathrm{i}\boldsymbol{\rho}\cdot \mathbf{r}}\mathrm{d}\lambda\mathrm{d}\mu\mathrm{d}\nu \end{align}\]

这里向量 \(\mathbf{r} = (x,y,z), \boldsymbol{\rho} = (\lambda,\mu,\nu)\) 。以 \(\mathbf{r}\) 方向为极轴方向取球坐标， \(r=\sqrt{x^{y}+y^{2}+z^{2}}\) ，则

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} U(t,x,y,z) &= \frac{1}{(2\pi)^{3}} \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\frac{\sin a\rho t}{a\rho} \int_{0}^{2\pi}\int_{0}^{\pi} e^{\mathrm{i}\rho r\cos\theta}\rho^{2}\sin\theta\mathrm{d}\theta\mathrm{d}\varphi\mathrm{d}\rho \\ &= -\frac{1}{4\pi^{2}a} \int_{0}^{+\infty} \sin a\rho t \frac{e^{\mathrm{i}\rho r\cos\theta}}{\mathrm{i}r}\Big|_{0}^{\pi}\mathrm{d}\rho \\ &= \frac{1}{2\pi^{2}ar} \int_{0}^{+\infty} \sin a\rho t \sin \rho r \mathrm{d}\rho \\ &= \frac{1}{4\pi^{2}ar} \int_{0}^{+\infty} [\cos \rho(r-at) - \cos\rho(r+at)]\mathrm{d}\rho \\ &= \frac{1}{8\pi^{2}ar} \int_{-\infty}^{\infty} \Big[ e^{\mathrm{i}\rho(r-at)} - e^{\mathrm{i}\rho(r + at)} \Big]\mathrm{d}\rho \\ &= \frac{1}{4\pi ar} [\delta(r-at) - \delta(r+at)] \\ &= \frac{\delta(r-at)}{4\pi ar} \end{align}\end{split}\]

根据该基本解，可以得知三维波动方程初值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \cfrac{\partial^{2}u}{\partial t^{2}} = a^{2}\Delta_{3}u + f(t,x,y,z) ,\quad t>0, -\infty<x,y,z<+\infty \\ u|_{t=0} = \varphi(x,y,z) ,\quad \cfrac{\partial u}{\partial t}\Big|_{t=0} = \psi(x,y,z) \end{array} \right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

的解为

\[\begin{align} u(t,M) = U(t,M) * \psi(M) + \frac{\partial}{\partial t}[U(t,M) * \varphi(M)] + \int_{0}^{t}U(t-\tau, M) * f(\tau,M)\mathrm{d}\tau ,\quad M=(x,y,z)\in\mathbb{R}^{3} \end{align}\]

其中

\[\begin{align} u_{1}(t,x,y,z) = U(t,M) * \psi(M) = \frac{1}{4\pi a}\iiint\limits_{-\infty}^{+\infty} \frac{\delta(r-at)}{r}\psi(\xi,\eta,\zeta)\mathrm{d}\xi\mathrm{d}\eta\mathrm{d}\zeta ,\quad r = \sqrt{(x-\xi)^{2} + (y-\eta)^{2} + (z-\zeta)^{2}} \end{align}\]

如果以 \(M=(x,y,z)\) 为中心， \(r\) 为半径作球面 \(S_{r}\) ，球坐标变换 \(\xi = x + r\sin\theta\cos\varphi\) ， \(\eta = y + r\sin\theta\sin\varphi\) ， \(\zeta = z + r\cos\theta\) ，则

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} u_{1}(t,x,y,z) &= \frac{1}{4\pi a} \int_{0}^{+\infty} \frac{\delta(r-at)}{r} \Big[ \oint_{S_{r}}\psi(\xi,\eta,\zeta)\mathrm{d}S \Big]\mathrm{d}r \\ &= \frac{1}{4\pi a^{2}t} \oint_{S_{at}}\psi(\xi,\eta,\zeta)\mathrm{d}S \\ &= t \cdot \frac{1}{4\pi(at)^{2}}\oint_{S_{at}}\psi(\xi,\eta,\zeta)\mathrm{d}S \\ &= tM_{at}(\psi) \end{align}\end{split}\]

其中，记号 \(M_{at}(\psi)\) 表示函数 \(\psi\) 在以 \((x,y,z)\) 为中心， \(at\) 为半径的球面 \(S_{at}\) 上的平均值。类似地，可以得到

\[\begin{align} u_{2}(t,x,y,z) = \frac{\partial }{\partial t}U(t,M) * \varphi(M) = \frac{\partial }{\partial t}[tM_{at}(\varphi)] \end{align}\]
\[\begin{split}\begin{align} u_{3}(t,x,y,z) &= \int_{0}^{t} U(t-\tau,M) * f(\tau,M)\mathrm{d}\tau \\ &= \int_{0}^{t}(t-\tau)M_{a(t-\tau)}(f)\mathrm{d}\tau \\ &= \int_{0}^{t}\frac{1}{4\pi a^{2}(t-\tau)}\oint_{S_{a(t-\tau)}}f(\tau,\xi,\eta,\zeta)\mathrm{d}S\mathrm{d}\tau \\ &= \frac{1}{4\pi a^{2}}\int_{0}^{at} \oint_{S_{r}}\frac{f(t-\frac{r}{a}, \xi,\eta,\zeta)}{r}\mathrm{d}S\mathrm{d}r \end{align}\end{split}\]

最后一步由变量代换 \(r=a(t-\tau)\) 得到，公式中的球面 \(S_{a(t-\tau)}\) 和 \(S_{r}\) 均以 \((x,y,z)\) 为中心。

特别的，齐次三维波动方程初值问题的解为

\[\begin{align} u(t,x,y,z) = tM_{at}(\psi) + \frac{\partial }{\partial t}[tM_{at}(\varphi)] \end{align}\]

注解

利用降维法求解二位波动方程初值问题

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \cfrac{\partial^{2}u}{\partial t^{2}} = a^{2}\Big( \cfrac{\partial^{2}u}{\partial x^{2}} + \cfrac{\partial^{2}u}{\partial y^{2}} \Big) ,\quad t>0, -\infty<x,y<+\infty \\ u|_{t=0} = \varphi(x,y) ,\quad \cfrac{\partial u}{\partial t}\Big|_{t=0} = \psi(x,y) \end{array} \right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

该二维问题可以看成是三维波动方程当初始条件 \(u|_{t=0} = \varphi(x,y), \frac{\partial u}{\partial t}\Big|_{t=0} = \psi(x,y)\) 时的特殊情况。于是可知

\[\begin{align} u(t,x,y) = tM_{at}(\psi) + \frac{\partial}{\partial t}[tM_{at}(\varphi)] \end{align}\]

首先需要将 \(M_{at}(\psi)\) 中的球面积分化为二重积分。由于被积函数 \(\psi(\xi,\eta)\) 与 \(\zeta\) 无关， \(\psi\) 在上、下半球面上的积分值相同。上半球面的方程为

\[\begin{align} \zeta = z + \sqrt{(at)^{2} - (\xi - x)^{2} - (\eta - y)^{2}} \end{align}\]

球面面积元 \(\mathrm{d}S\) 与其在 \(\xi-\eta\) 平面的投影 \(\mathrm{d}A\) 之间存在关系

\[\begin{align} \mathrm{d}S = \sqrt{1 + \Big(\frac{\partial \zeta}{\partial \xi}\Big)^{2} + \Big(\frac{\partial \zeta}{\partial \eta}\Big)^{2}} \mathrm{d}A = \frac{at}{\sqrt{(at)^{2} - (\xi-x)^{2} - (\eta - y)^{2}}}\mathrm{d}A \end{align}\]

所以

\[\begin{align} \oint_{S_{at}}\psi(\xi,\eta)\mathrm{d}S = 2\iint_{S_{at}^{up}}\psi(\xi,\eta)\mathrm{d}S = 2at\iint_{D_{at}}\frac{\psi(\xi,\eta)}{\sqrt{(at)^{2} - (\xi-x)^{2} - (\eta - y)^{2}}}\mathrm{d}A \end{align}\]

其中二重积分区域 \(D_{at}\) 是 \(S_{at}\) 在 \(\xi-\eta\) 平面上的投影，即以 \((x,y)\) 为中心， \(at\) 为半径的圆域。所以二维波动方程初值问题式的解为

\[\begin{align} u(t,x,y) = \frac{1}{2\pi a} \iint_{D_{at}}\frac{\psi(\xi,\eta)}{\sqrt{(at)^{2} - (\xi-x)^{2} - (\eta - y)^{2}}}\mathrm{d}\xi\mathrm{d}\eta + \frac{1}{2\pi a}\frac{\partial }{\partial t} \iint_{D_{at}}\frac{\psi(\xi,\eta)}{\sqrt{(at)^{2} - (\xi-x)^{2} - (\eta - y)^{2}}}\mathrm{d}\xi\mathrm{d}\eta \end{align}\]

特别的，如果取 \(\varphi(x,y) = 0, \psi(x,y) = \delta(x,y)\) ，根据上式可以得到二位波动方程初值问题的基本解

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} U(t,x,y) &= \frac{1}{2\pi a} \iint_{D_{at}}\frac{\delta(\xi,\eta)}{\sqrt{(at)^{2} - (\xi-x)^{2} - (\eta - y)^{2}}}\mathrm{d}\xi\mathrm{d}\eta \\ &= \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \cfrac{1}{2\pi a \sqrt{(at)^{2} - x^{2} - y^{2}}} ,\quad r<at \\ 0 ,\quad r>at \end{array} \right. \\ &= \frac{1}{2\pi a \sqrt{(at)^{2} - r^{2}}}H(at - r) ,\quad r=\sqrt{x^{2} + y^{2}} \end{align}\end{split}\]

Notions on Hyperbolic Partial Differential Equations¶

In this chapter we study some elementary properties of a class of hyperbolic Partial Differential Equations. Here we deal almost exclusively with hyperbolic PDEs and hyperbolic conservation laws in particular. There are three main reasons for this: (1) The equations of compressible fluid flow reduce to hyperbolic systems, the Euler equations, when the effects of viscosity and heat conduction are neglected. (2) Numerically, it is generally accepted that the hyperbolic terms of the PDEs of fluid flow are the terms that pose the most stringent requirements on the discretisation techniques. (3) The theory of hyperbolic systems is much more advanced than that for more complete mathematical models, such as the Navier-Stokes equations. In addition, there has in recent years been a noticeable increase in research and development activities centred on the theme of hyperbolic problems, as these cover a wide range of areas of scientific and technological interest.

Quasi-Linear Equations: Basic Concepts¶

In this section we study systems of first-order partial differential equations of the form

\[\begin{align} \frac{\partial u_{i}}{\partial t} + \sum_{j=1}^{m} a_{ij}(x,t,u_{1},\cdots,u_{m})\frac{\partial u_{j}}{\partial x} + b_{i}(x,t,u_{1},\cdots,u_{m}) = 0 \end{align}\]

for \(i=1,\cdots,m\) . This is a system of \(m\) equations in \(m\) unknowns \(u_{i}\) that depend on space \(x\) and a time-like variable \(t\) . Here \(u_{i}\) are the dependent variables and \(x,t\) are the independent variables; this is expressed via the notation \(u_{i}=u_{i}(x,t)\) ; \(\partial u_{i}/\partial t\) denotes the partial derivative of \(u_{i}(x,t)\) with respect to \(t\) ; similarly \(\partial u_{i} / \partial x\) denotes the partial derivative of \(u_{i}(x,t)\) with respect to \(t\) ; similarly \(\partial u_{i}/\partial t\) denotes the partial derivative of \(u_{i}(x,t)\) with respect to \(x\) . We also make use of subscripts to denote partial derivatives. The system can also be written in matrix form as

\[\begin{align} \mathbf{U}_{t} + \mathbf{A}\mathbf{U}_{x} + \mathbf{B} = \mathbf{0} \end{align}\]

with

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \mathbf{U} = \begin{bmatrix} u_{1} \\ u_{2} \\ \vdots \\ u_{m} \end{bmatrix} ,\quad \mathbf{B} = \begin{bmatrix} b_{1} \\ b_{2} \\ \vdots \\ b_{m} \end{bmatrix} ,\quad \mathbf{A} = \begin{bmatrix} a_{11} & \cdots & a_{1m} \\ a_{21} & \cdots & a_{2m} \\ \vdots & \vdots & \vdots \\ a_{m1} & \cdots & a_{mm} \end{bmatrix} \end{align}\end{split}\]

If the entries \(a_{ij}\) of the matrix \(\mathbf{A}\) are all constant and the component \(b_{j}\) of the vector \(\mathbf{B}\) are also constant ten system is linear with constant coefficients. If \(a_{ij}=a_{ij}(x,t)\) and \(b_{i}=b_{i}(x,t)\) the system is linear with variable coefficients. The system is still linear if \(\mathbf{B}\) depends linearly on \(\mathbf{U}\) and is called quasi-linear if the coefficient matrix \(\mathbf{A}\) is a function of the vector \(\mathbf{U}\) , that is \(\mathbf{A}=\mathbf{A}(\mathbf{A})\) . Note that quasi-linear systems are in general systems of non-linear equations. The system is called homogeneous if \(\mathbf{B}=\mathbf{0}\) . For a set of PDEs of the form, one needs to specify the range of variation of the independent variables \(x\) and \(t\) . Usually \(x\) lies in a subinterval of the real line, namely \(x_{l}<x<x_{r}\) ; the values \(x_{l},x_{r}\) one also needs to specify Boundary Conditions (BCs). In this Chapter we assume the domain is the full real line, \(-\infty < x < \infty\) , and thus no boundary conditions need to be specified. As to variations of time we assume \(t_{0} < t < \infty\) . An Initial Condition (IC) needs to be specified at the initial time, which is usually chosen to be \(t_{0}=0\) .

Two scalar \((m=1)\) examples of PDEs of the form are the liear advection equation

\[\begin{align} \frac{\partial u}{\partial t} + a\frac{\partial u}{\partial x} = 0 \end{align}\]

and the inviscid Burgers equation

\[\begin{align} \frac{\partial u}{\partial t} + u\frac{\partial u}{\partial x} = 0 \end{align}\]

In the linear advection equation the coefficient \(a\) (a constant) is the wave propagation speed. In the Burgers equation \(a=a(u)=u\) .

Conservation lawss are systems of partial differential equations that can be written in the form

\[\begin{align} \mathbf{U}_{t} + \mathbf{F}(\mathbf{U})_{x} = \mathbf{0} \end{align}\]

where

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \mathbf{U} = \begin{bmatrix} u_{1} \\ u_{2} \\ \vdots \\ u_{m} \end{bmatrix} ,\quad \mathbf{F}(\mathbf{U}) = \begin{bmatrix} f_{1} \\ f_{2} \\ \vdots \\ f_{m} \end{bmatrix} \end{align}\end{split}\]

\(\mathbf{U}\) is called the vector of conserved variables, \(\mathbf{F}=\mathbf{F}(\mathbf{U})\) is the vector of fluxes and each of its components \(f_{i}\) is a function of the components \(u_{j}\) of \(\mathbf{U}\) .

The Jacobian of the flux function \(\mathbf{F}(\mathbf{U})\) in the above systems is the matrix

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \mathbf{A}(\mathbf{U}) = \frac{\partial \mathbf{F}}{\partial \mathbf{U}} = \begin{bmatrix} \frac{\partial f_{1}}{\partial u_{1}} & \cdots & \frac{\partial f_{1}}{\partial u_{m}} \\ \frac{\partial f_{2}}{\partial u_{1}} & \cdots & \frac{\partial f_{2}}{\partial u_{m}} \\ \vdots & \vdots & \vdots \\ \frac{\partial f_{m}}{\partial u_{1}} & \cdots & \frac{\partial f_{m}}{\partial u_{m}} \end{bmatrix} \end{align}\end{split}\]

The entries \(a_{ij}\) of \(\mathbf{A}(\mathbf{U})\) are partial derivatives of the components \(f_{i}\) of the vector \(\mathbf{F}\) with respect to the components \(u_{j}\) of conserved variables \(\mathbf{U}\) , that is \(a_{ij}=\partial f_{i} / \partial u_{j}\) .

Note that conservation laws of the form can also be written in quasi-linear form, with \(\mathbf{B}\equiv\mathbf{0}\) , by applying the chain rule to the second term in the conservation laws, namely

\[\begin{align} \frac{\partial \mathbf{F}(\mathbf{U})}{\partial x} = \frac{\partial \mathbf{F}}{\partial \mathbf{U}}\frac{\partial \mathbf{U}}{\partial x} \end{align}\]

Hence the conservation laws becomes

\[\begin{align} \mathbf{U}_{t} + \mathbf{A}(\mathbf{U})\mathbf{U}_{x} = \mathbf{0} \end{align}\]

The scalar PDEs, the linear advection equation and the inviscid Burgers equation, can be expressed as conservation laws, namely

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} & \frac{\partial u}{\partial t} + \frac{\partial f(u)}{\partial x} = 0 ,\quad f(u) = au \\ & \frac{\partial u}{\partial t} + \frac{\partial f(u)}{\partial x} = 0 ,\quad f(u) = \frac{1}{2}u^{2} \end{align}\end{split}\]

Physically, eigenvalues represent speeds of propagation of information. Speeds will be measured positive in the direction of increasing \(x\) and negative otherwise.

For the scalar examples above, the eigenvalues are trivially found to be \(\lambda = a\) and \(\lambda = u\) respectively. Next we find eigenvalues and eigenvectors for a system of PDEs.

The linearised equations of Gas Dynamics are the \(2 \times 2\) linear system

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} & \frac{\partial \rho}{\partial t} + \rho_{0}\frac{\partial u}{\partial x} = 0 \\ & \frac{\partial u}{\partial t} + \frac{a^{2}}{\rho_{0}}\frac{\partial \rho}{\partial x} = 0 \end{align}\end{split}\]

where the unkowns are the density \(u_{1} = \rho(x,t)\) and the speed \(u_{2}=u(x,t)\) ; \(\rho_{0}\) is a constant reference density and \(a\) is the sound speed, a positive constant. When written in the matrix form this system reads

\[\begin{align} \mathbf{U}_{t} + \mathbf{A}\mathbf{U}_{x} = \mathbf{0} \end{align}\]

with

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \mathbf{U} = \begin{bmatrix} \rho \\ u \end{bmatrix} ,\quad \mathbf{A} = \begin{bmatrix} 0 & \rho_{0} \\ a^{2}/\rho_{0} & 0 \end{bmatrix} \end{align}\end{split}\]

The eigenvalues of the system are the zeros of the characteristic polynomial

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} |\mathbf{A} - \lambda\mathbf{I}| = \det \begin{bmatrix} 0-\lambda & \rho_{0} \\ a^{2}/\rho_{0} & 0-\lambda \end{bmatrix} \end{align}\end{split}\]

That is, \(\lambda^{2}=a^{2}\) , which has two real and distinct solutions, namely

\[\begin{align} \lambda_{1}=-a ,\quad \lambda_{2}=+a \end{align}\]

We now can find the right eigenvectors \(\mathbf{K}^{(1)}, \mathbf{K}^{(2)}\) corresponding to the eigenvalues \(\lambda_{1}\) and \(\lambda_{2}\) , namely

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \mathbf{K}^{(1)} = \begin{bmatrix} \rho_{0} \\ -a \end{bmatrix} ,\quad \mathbf{K}^{(2)} = \begin{bmatrix} \rho_{0} \\ a \end{bmatrix} \end{align}\end{split}\]

A system of first-order partial differential equations is said to be hyperbolic at a point \((x,t)\) if \(\mathbf{A}\) has \(m\) real eigenvalues \(\lambda_{1},\cdots,\lambda_{m}\) and a corresponding set of \(m\) linearly independent right eigenvectors \(\mathbf{K}^{(1)}, \cdots, \mathbf{K}^{(m)}\) . The system is said to be strictly hyperbolic if the eigenvalues \(\lambda_{i}\) are all distinct.

Note that strict hyperbolicity implies hyperbolicity, because real and distinct eigenvalues ensure the existence of a set of linearly independent eigenvectors. The system is said to be elliptic at a point \((x,t)\) if none of the eigenvalues \(\lambda_{i}\) of \(\mathbf{A}\) are real. Both scalar examples given above are trivially hyperbolic. The linearised gas dynamic equations are also hyperbolic, since \(\lambda_{1}\) and \(\lambda_{2}\) are both real at any point \((x,t)\) . Moreover, as the eigenvalues are also distinct this system is strictly hyperbolic.

An example of a first-order system of the form with \(t\) replaced by \(x\) and \(x\) replaced by \(y\) is the Cauchy-Riemann equations

\[\begin{align} \frac{\partial u}{\partial x} - \frac{\partial v}{\partial y} = 0 ,\quad \frac{\partial v}{\partial x} + \frac{\partial u}{\partial y} = 0 \end{align}\]

where \(u_{1}=u(x,y)\) and \(u_{2}=v(x,y)\) . These equations arise in the study of analytic in Complex Analysis. When written in matrix notation, equations become

\[\begin{align} \mathbf{U}_{x} + \mathbf{A}\mathbf{U}_{y} = \mathbf{0} \end{align}\]

with

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \mathbf{U} = \begin{bmatrix} u \\ v \end{bmatrix} ,\quad \mathbf{A} = \begin{bmatrix} 0 & - 1 \\ 1 & 0 \end{bmatrix} \end{align}\end{split}\]

The charateristic polynomial \(|\mathbf{A} - \lambda\mathbf{I}| = 0\) gives \(\lambda^{2}+1=0\) , which has no real solutions for \(\lambda\) and thus the system is elliptic.

The small perturbation steady equations were introduced

\[\begin{align} u_{x} - a^{2}v_{y} = 0 ,\quad v_{x} - u_{y} = 0 \end{align}\]

with

\[\begin{align} a^{2} = \frac{1}{M_{\infty}^{2} - 1} \end{align}\]

\(M_{\infty} = \text{constant}\) denotes the free-stream Mach number and \(u(x,y),v(x,y)\) are small perturbations of the \(x\) and \(y\) velocity components respectively. In matrix notation these equations read

\[\begin{align} \mathbf{U}_{x} + \mathbf{A}\mathbf{U}_{y} = \mathbf{0} \end{align}\]

with

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \mathbf{U} = \begin{bmatrix} u \\ v \end{bmatrix} ,\quad \mathbf{A} = \begin{bmatrix} 0 & -a^{2} \\ -1 & 0 \end{bmatrix} \end{align}\end{split}\]

The character of these equations depends entirely on the value of the Mach number \(M_{\infty}\) . For subsonic flow \(M_{\infty} < 1\) the characteristic polynomial has complex solutions and thus the equations are of elliptic type. For supersonic flow \(M_{\infty} > 1\) and the system is strictly hyperbolic, wich eigenvalues

\[\begin{align} \lambda_{1} = -a ,\quad \lambda_{2} = +a \end{align}\]

We can check that the corresponding right eigenvectors are

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} \mathbf{K}^{(1)} = \begin{bmatrix} a \\ 1 \end{bmatrix} ,\quad \mathbf{K}^{(2)} = \begin{bmatrix} a \\ -1 \end{bmatrix} \end{align}\end{split}\]

The Linear Advection Equation¶

A general, time-dependent linear advection equation in three space dimensions reads

\[\begin{align} u_{t} + a(x,y,z,t)u_{x} + b(x,y,z,t)u_{y} + c(x,y,z,t)u_{z} = 0 \end{align}\]

where the unkown is \(u=u(x,y,z,t)\) and \(a,b,c\) are variable coefficients. If the coefficients are sufficiently smooth one can express the equation as a conservation law with some terms, namely

\[\begin{align} u_{t} + (au)_{x} + (bu)_{y} + (cu)_{z} = u(a_{x} + b_{y} + c_{z}) \end{align}\]

In this section we study in detial the initial-value problem (IVP) for the special case of the linear advection equation, namely

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} & u_{t} + au_{x} = 0 ,\quad -\infty < x < \infty , t>0 \\ & u(x,0) = u_{0}(x) \end{align}\end{split}\]

where \(a\) is a constant wave propagation speed. The initial data at time \(t=0\) is a function of \(x\) alone and is denoted by \(u_{0}(x)\) . Generally, we shall not explicit about the conditions \(-\infty < x < \infty\) ; \(t>0\) on the independent variables when stating an initial-value problem. The PDE above is the simplest hyperboli PDE and is also the simplest hyperbolic conservation law. It is a very useful model equation for the purpose of studying numerical methods for hyperbolic conservation laws, in the same way as the linear, first-order ordinary differential equation

\[\begin{align} \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{d}t} = \beta ,\quad x=x(t), \quad \beta=\text{constant} \end{align}\]

is a popular model equation for analysing numerical methods for Ordinary Differential Equation (ODEs). We study numerical methods for ODEs in connection with source terms in inhomogeneous PDEs.

We recall the definition of characteristics or characteristic curves in the context of a scalar equation. Characteristics may be defined as curves \(x=x(t)\) in the t-x plane along which the PDE becomes an ODE. Consider \(x=x(t)\) and regard \(u\) as a function of \(t\) , that is \(u=u(x(t),t)\) . The rate of change of \(u\) along \(x=x(t)\) is

\[\begin{align} \frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{d}t} = \frac{\partial u}{\partial t} + \frac{\mathrm{d} x}{\mathrm{d} t}\frac{\partial u}{\partial x} \end{align}\]

If the characteristic curve \(x=x(t)\) satisfies the ODE

\[\begin{align} \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{d}t} = a \end{align}\]

then the PDE \(u_{t}+au_{x}=0\) , together with \(\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{d}t} = \frac{\partial u}{\partial t} + \frac{\mathrm{d} x}{\mathrm{d} t}\frac{\partial u}{\partial x}\) and \(\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{d}t} = a\) , gives

\[\begin{align} \frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{d}t} = \frac{\partial u}{\partial t} + a\frac{\partial u}{\partial x} = 0 \end{align}\]

Therefore the rate of change of \(u\) along the characteristic curve \(x=x(t)\) satisfying \(\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{d}t}=a\) is zero, that is, \(u\) is constant along the curve \(x=x(t)\) . The speed \(a\) in \(\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{d}t}=a\) is called the characteristic speed and according to \(\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{d}t}=a\) it is the slope of the curve \(x=x(t)\) in the t-x plane. In practice it is more common to use the x-t plane to sketch the characteristics, in which case the slope of the curves in question is \(1/a\) . The family of characteristic curves \(x=x(t)\) given by the ODE \(\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{d}t}=a\) are illustrated in Fig.2.1 for \(a>0\) and are a one-parameter family of curves. A particular member of this family is determined when an initial condition (IC) at time \(t=0\) for the ODE is added. Suppose we set

\[\begin{align} x(0) = x_{0} \end{align}\]

then the single characteristic curve that passes through the point \((x_{0},0)\) , according to \(\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{d}t}=a\) is

\[\begin{align} x = x_{0} + at \end{align}\]

This is also illustrated in Fig.2.1. Now we may regard the initial position \(x_{0}\) as a parameter and in this way we reproduce the full one-parameter family of characteristics. The fact that the curves are parallel is typical of linear hyperbolic PDEs with constant coefficients.

Recall the conclusion from \(\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{d}t}=\frac{\partial u}{\partial t} + a\frac{\partial u}{\partial x}=0\) that \(u\) remains constant along characteristics. Thus, if \(u\) is given the initial value \(u(x,0)=u_{0}(x)\) at time \(t=0\) , then along the whole characteristic curve \(x(t)=x_{0}+at\) that passes through the initial point \(x_{0}\) on the x-axis, the solution is

\[\begin{align} u(x,t) = u_{0}(x_{0}) = u_{0}(x-at) \end{align}\]

The second equality follows from \(x=x_{0}+at\) . The interpretation of the solution of the PDE is this: given an initial profile \(u_{0}(x)\) , the PDE will simply translate this profile with velocity \(a\) to the right if \(a>0\) and to the left if \(a<0\) . The shape of the initial profile remains unchanged. The model equation \(u_{t}+au_{x}=0\) under study contains some of the basic features of wave propagation phenomena, where a wave is understood as some recognisable feature of a disturbance that travels at a finite speed.

By using geometric arguments, we have constructed the analytical solution of the general IVP for the linear advection equation. This is given by \(u(x,t)=u_{0}(x_{0})=u_{0}(x-at)\) in terms of the initial data \(u_{0}(x)\) . Now we study a special IVP called the Riemann problem

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} & u_{t} + au_{x} = 0 \\ & u(x,0) = u_{0}(x) = \left\{ \begin{array}{ll} u_{L} \quad \text{if}~x<0 \\ u_{R} \quad \text{if}~x>0 \end{array} \right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

where \(u_{L}\) and \(u_{R}\) are two constant values, as shown in Fig.2.2. Note that the initial data has a discontinuity at \(x=0\) . The IVP above is the simplest initial-value problem one can pose. The trivial case would result when \(u_{L}=u_{R}\) . From the previous discussion on the solution of the general IVP, we expect any point on the initial profile to propagate a distance \(d=at\) in time \(t\) . In particular, we expect the initial discontinuity at \(x=0\) to propagate a distance \(d=at\) in time \(t\) . This particular characteristic curve \(x=at\) will then separate those characteristic curves to the left, on which the solution takes on the value \(u_{L}\) , from those curves to the right, on which the solution takes on the value \(u_{R}\) ; see Fig.2.3. So the solution of the Riemann problem is simply

\[\begin{split}\begin{align} u(x,t) = u_{0}(x-at) = \left\{ \begin{array}{ll} u_{L} \quad \text{if}~x-at<0 \\ u_{R} \quad \text{if}~x-at>0 \end{array} \right. \end{align}\end{split}\]

The solution also follows directly from the general solution, namely \(u(x,t)=u_{0}(x-at)\) . From the Riemann problem IC, \(u_{0}(x-at)=u_{L}\) if \(x-at<0\) and \(u_{0}(x-at)=u_{R}\) if \(x-at>0\) . The solution of the Riemann problem can be represented in the x-t plane, as shown in Fig.2.3. Through any point \(x_{0}\) on the x-axis one can draw a characteristic. As \(a\) is constant these are all parallel to each other. For the solution of the Riemann problem the characteristic that passes through \(x=0\) is significant. This is the only one across which the solution changes.

Linear Hyperbolic Systems¶

In the previous section we studied in detial the behaviour and the general solution of the simplest PDE of hyperbolic type, namely the linear advection equation with constant wave propagation speed. Here we extend the analysis to sets of \(m\) hyperbolic PDEs of the form

\[\begin{align} \mathbf{U}_{t} + \mathbf{A}\mathbf{U}_{x} = \mathbf{0} \end{align}\]

where the coefficient matrix \(\mathbf{A}\) is constant. From the assumption of hyperbolicity \(\mathbf{A}\) has \(m\) real eigenvalues \(\lambda_{i}\) and \(m\) linearly independent eigenvectors \(\mathbf{K}^{(i)}, i=1,\cdots,m\) .
